directory.\n   222→func (c *LeveledCompactor) Plan(dir string) ([]string, error) {\n   223→\tdirs, err := blockDirs(dir)\n   224→\tif err != nil {\n   225→\t\treturn nil, err\n   226→\t}\n   227→\tif len(dirs) < 1 {\n   228→\t\treturn nil, nil\n   229→\t}\n   230→\n   231→\tvar dms []dirMeta\n   232→\tfor _, dir := range dirs {\n   233→\t\tmeta, _, err := readMetaFile(dir)\n   234→\t\tif err != nil {\n   235→\t\t\treturn nil, err\n   236→\t\t}\n   237→\t\tdms = append(dms, dirMeta{dir, meta})\n   238→\t}\n   239→\treturn c.plan(dms)\n   240→}\n   241→\n   242→func (c *LeveledCompactor) plan(dms []dirMeta) ([]string, error) {\n   243→\tslices.SortFunc(dms, func(a, b dirMeta) int {\n   244→\t\tswitch {\n   245→\t\tcase a.meta.MinTime < b.meta.MinTime:\n   246→\t\t\treturn -1\n   247→\t\tcase a.meta.MinTime > b.meta.MinTime:\n   248→\t\t\treturn 1\n   249→\t\tdefault:\n   250→\t\t\treturn 0\n   251→\t\t}\n   252→\t})\n   253→\n   254→\tres := c.selectOverlappingDirs(dms)\n   255→\tif len(res) > 0 {\n   256→\t\treturn res, nil\n   257→\t}\n   258→\t// No overlapping blocks, do compaction the usual way.\n   259→\t// We do not include a recently created block with max(minTime), so the block which was just created from WAL.\n   260→\t// This gives users a window of a full block size to piece-wise backup new data without having to care about data overlap.\n   261→\tdms = dms[:len(dms)-1]\n   262→\n   263→\tfor _, dm := range c.selectDirs(dms) {\n   264→\t\tres = append(res, dm.dir)\n   265→\t}\n   266→\tif len(res) > 0 {\n   267→\t\treturn res, nil\n   268→\t}\n   269→\n   270→\t// Compact any blocks with big enough time range that have >5% tombstones.\n   271→\tfor i := len(dms) - 1; i >= 0; i-- {\n   272→\t\tmeta := dms[i].meta\n   273→\t\tif meta.MaxTime-meta.MinTime < c.ranges[len(c.ranges)/2] {\n   274→\t\t\t// If the block is entirely deleted, then we don't care about the block being big enough.\n   275→\t\t\t// TODO: This is assuming single tombstone is for distinct series, which might be no true.\n   276→\t\t\tif meta.Stats.NumTombstones > 0 && meta.Stats.NumTombstones >= meta.Stats.NumSeries {\n   277→\t\t\t\treturn []string{dms[i].dir}, nil\n   278→\t\t\t}\n   279→\t\t\tbreak\n   280→\t\t}\n   281→\t\tif float64(meta.Stats.NumTombstones)/float64(meta.Stats.NumSeries+1) > 0.05 {\n   282→\t\t\treturn []string{dms[i].dir}, nil\n   283→\t\t}\n   284→\t}\n   285→\n   286→\treturn nil, nil\n   287→}\n   288→\n   289→// selectDirs returns the dir metas that should be compacted into a single new block.\n   290→// If only a single block range is configured, the result is always nil.\n   291→func (c *LeveledCompactor) selectDirs(ds []dirMeta) []dirMeta {\n   292→\tif len(c.ranges) < 2 || len(ds) < 1 {\n   293→\t\treturn nil\n   294→\t}\n   295→\n   296→\thighTime := ds[len(ds)-1].meta.MinTime\n   297→\n   298→\tfor _, iv := range c.ranges[1:] {\n   299→\t\tparts := splitByRange(ds, iv)\n   300→\t\tif len(parts) == 0 {\n   301→\t\t\tcontinue\n   302→\t\t}\n   303→\n   304→\tOuter:\n   305→\t\tfor _, p := range parts {\n   306→\t\t\t// Do not select the range if it has a block whose compaction failed.\n   307→\t\t\tfor _, dm := range p {\n   308→\t\t\t\tif dm.meta.Compaction.Failed {\n   309→\t\t\t\t\tcontinue Outer\n   310→\t\t\t\t}\n   311→\t\t\t}\n   312→\n   313→\t\t\tmint := p[0].meta.MinTime\n   314→\t\t\tmaxt := p[len(p)-1].meta.MaxTime\n   315→\t\t\t// Pick the range of blocks if it spans the full range (potentially with gaps)\n   316→\t\t\t// or is before the most recent block.\n   317→\t\t\t// This ensures we don't compact blocks prematurely when another one of the same\n   318→\t\t\t// size still fits in the range.\n   319→\t\t\tif (maxt-mint == iv || maxt <= highTime) && len(p) > 1 {\n   320→\t\t\t\treturn p\n   321→\t\t\t}\n   322→\t\t}\n   323→\t}\n   324→\n   325→\treturn nil\n   326→}\n   327→\n   328→// selectOverlappingDirs returns all dirs with overlapping time ranges.\n   329→// It expects sorted input by mint and returns the overlapping dirs in the same order as received.\n   330→func (c *LeveledCompactor) selectOverlappingDirs(ds []dirMeta) []string {\n   331→\tif !c.enableOverlappingCompaction {\n   332→\t\treturn nil\n   333→\t}\n   334→\tif len(ds) < 2 {\n   335→\t\treturn nil\n   336→\t}\n   337→\tvar overlappingDirs []string\n   338→\tglobalMaxt := ds[0].meta.MaxTime\n   339→\tfor i, d := range ds[1:] {\n   340→\t\tif d.meta.MinTime < globalMaxt {\n   341→\t\t\tif len(overlappingDirs) == 0 { // When it is the first overlap, need to add the last one as well.\n   342→\t\t\t\toverlappingDirs = append(overlappingDirs, ds[i].dir)\n   343→\t\t\t}\n   344→\t\t\toverlappingDirs = append(overlappingDirs, d.dir)\n   345→\t\t} else if len(overlappingDirs) > 0 {\n   346→\t\t\tbreak\n   347→\t\t}\n   348→\t\tif d.meta.MaxTime > globalMaxt {\n   349→\t\t\tglobalMaxt = d.meta.MaxTime\n   350→\t\t}\n   351→\t}\n   352→\treturn overlappingDirs\n   353→}\n   354→\n   355→// splitByRange splits the directories by the time range. The range sequence starts at 0.\n   356→//\n   357→// For example, if we have blocks [0-10, 10-20, 50-60, 90-100] and the split range tr is 30\n   358→// it returns [0-10, 10-20], [50-60], [90-100].\n   359→func splitByRange(ds []dirMeta, tr int64) [][]dirMeta {\n   360→\tvar splitDirs [][]dirMeta\n   361→\n   362→\tfor i := 0; i < len(ds); {\n   363→\t\tvar (\n   364→\t\t\tgroup []dirMeta\n   365→\t\t\tt0    int64\n   366→\t\t\tm     = ds[i].meta\n   367→\t\t)\n   368→\t\t// Compute start of aligned time range of size tr closest to the current block's start.\n   369→\t\tif m.MinTime >= 0 {\n   370→\t\t\tt0 = tr * (m.MinTime / tr)\n   371→\t\t} else {\n   372→\t\t\tt0 = tr * ((m.MinTime - tr + 1) / tr)\n   373→\t\t}\n   374→\t\t// Skip blocks that don't fall into the range. This can happen via mis-alignment or\n   375→\t\t// by being the multiple of the intended range.\n   376→\t\tif m.MaxTime > t0+tr {\n   377→\t\t\ti++\n   378→\t\t\tcontinue\n   379→\t\t}\n   380→\n   381→\t\t// Add all dirs to the current group that are within [t0, t0+tr].\n   382→\t\tfor ; i < len(ds); i++ {\n   383→\t\t\t// Either the block falls into the next range or doesn't fit at all (checked above).\n   384→\t\t\tif ds[i].meta.MaxTime > t0+tr {\n   385→\t\t\t\tbreak\n   386→\t\t\t}\n   387→\t\t\tgroup = append(group, ds[i])\n   388→\t\t}\n   389→\n   390→\t\tif len(group) > 0 {\n   391→\t\t\tsplitDirs = append(splitDirs, group)\n   392→\t\t}\n   393→\t}\n   394→\n   395→\treturn splitDirs\n   396→}\n   397→\n   398→// CompactBlockMetas merges many block metas into one, combining it's source blocks together\n   399→// and adjusting compaction level. Min/Max time of result block meta covers all input blocks.\n   400→func CompactBlockMetas(uid ulid.ULID, blocks ...*BlockMeta) *BlockMeta {\n   401→\tres := &BlockMeta{\n   402→\t\tULID: uid,\n   403→\t}\n   404→\n   405→\tsources := map[ulid.ULID]struct{}{}\n   406→\tmint := blocks[0].MinTime\n   407→\tmaxt := blocks[0].MaxTime\n   408→\n   409→\tfor _, b := range blocks {\n   410→\t\tif b.MinTime < mint {\n   411→\t\t\tmint = b.MinTime\n   412→\t\t}\n   413→\t\tif b.MaxTime > maxt {\n   414→\t\t\tmaxt = b.MaxTime\n   415→\t\t}\n   416→\t\tif b.Compaction.Level > res.Compaction.Level {\n   417→\t\t\tres.Compaction.Level = b.Compaction.Level\n   418→\t\t}\n   419→\t\tfor _, s := range b.Compaction.Sources {\n   420→\t\t\tsources[s] = struct{}{}\n   421→\t\t}\n   422→\t\tres.Compaction.Parents = append(res.Compaction.Parents, BlockDesc{\n   423→\t\t\tULID:    b.ULID,\n   424→\t\t\tMinTime: b.MinTime,\n   425→\t\t\tMaxTime: b.MaxTime,\n   426→\t\t})\n   427→\t}\n   428→\tres.Compaction.Level++\n   429→\n   430→\tfor s := range sources {\n   431→\t\tres.Compaction.Sources = append(res.Compaction.Sources, s)\n   432→\t}\n   433→\tslices.SortFunc(res.Compaction.Sources, func(a, b ulid.ULID) int {\n   434→\t\treturn a.Compare(b)\n   435→\t})\n   436→\n   437→\tres.MinTime = mint\n   438→\tres.MaxTime = maxt\n   439→\treturn res\n   440→}\n   441→\n   442→// Compact creates a new block in the compactor's directory from the blocks in the\n   443→// provided directories.\n   444→func (c *LeveledCompactor) Compact(dest string, dirs []string, open []*Block) (uid ulid.ULID, err error) {\n   445→\treturn c.CompactWithBlockPopulator(dest, dirs, open, DefaultBlockPopulator{})\n   446→}\n   447→\n   448→func (c *LeveledCompactor) CompactWithBlockPopulator(dest string, dirs []string, open []*Block, blockPopulator BlockPopulator) (uid ulid.ULID, err error) {\n   449→\tvar (\n   450→\t\tblocks []BlockReader\n   451→\t\tbs     []*Block\n   452→\t\tmetas  []*BlockMeta\n   453→\t\tuids   []string\n   454→\t)\n   455→\tstart := time.Now()\n   456→\n   457→\tfor _, d := range dirs {\n   458→\t\tmeta, _, err := readMetaFile(d)\n   459→\t\tif err != nil {\n   460→\t\t\treturn uid, err\n   461→\t\t}\n   462→\n   463→\t\tvar b *Block\n   464→\n   465→\t\t// Use already open blocks if we can, to avoid\n   466→\t\t// having the index data in memory twice.\n   467→\t\tfor _, o := range open {\n   468→\t\t\tif meta.ULID == o.Meta().ULID {\n   469→\t\t\t\tb = o\n   470→\t\t\t\tbreak\n 486→\t\tuids = append(uids, meta.ULID.String())\n   487→\t}\n   488→\n   489→\tuid = ulid.MustNew(ulid.Now(), rand.Reader)\n   490→\n   491→\tmeta := CompactBlockMetas(uid, metas...)\n   492→\terr = c.write(dest, meta, blockPopulator, blocks...)\n   493→\tif err == nil {\n   494→\t\tif meta.Stats.NumSamples == 0 {\n   495→\t\t\tfor _, b := range bs {\n   496→\t\t\t\tb.meta.Compaction.Deletable = true\n   497→\t\t\t\tn, err := writeMetaFile(c.logger, b.dir, &b.meta)\n   498→\t\t\t\tif err != nil {\n   499→\t\t\t\t\tlevel.Error(c.logger).Log(\n   500→\t\t\t\t\t\t\"msg\", \"Failed to write fmt.Sprintf(\"%v\", uids),\n   511→\t\t\t\t\"duration\", time.Since(start),\n   512→\t\t\t)\n   513→\t\t} else {\n   514→\t\t\tlevel.Info(c.logger).Log(\n   515→\t\t\t\t\"msg\", \"compact blocks\",\n   516→\t\t\t\t\"count\", len(blocks),\n   517→\t\t\t\t\"mint\", meta.MinTime,\n   518→\t\t\t\t\"maxt\", meta.MaxTime,\n   519→\t\t\t\t\"ulid\", meta.ULID,\n   520→\t\t\t\t\"sources\", fmt.Sprintf(\"%v\", uids),\n   521→\t\t\t\t\"duration\", time.Since(start),\n   522→\t\t\t)\n   523→\t\t}\n   524→\t\treturn uid, nil\n   525→\t}\n   526→\n   527→\terrs := tsdb_errors.NewMulti(err)\n   528→\tif !errors.Is(err, context.Canceled) {\n   529→\t\tfor _, b := range bs {\n   530→\t\t\tif err := b.setCompactionFailed(); err != nil {\n   531→\t\t\t\terrs.Add(fmt.Errorf(\"setting compaction failed for block: %s: %w\", b.Dir(), err))\n   532→\t\t\t}\n   533→\t\t}\n   534→\t}\n   535→\n   536→\treturn uid, errs.Err()\n   537→}\n   538→\n   539→func (c *LeveledCompactor) Write(dest string, b BlockReader, mint, maxt int64, base *BlockMeta) (ulid.ULID, error) {\n   540→\tstart := time.Now()\n   541→\n   542→\tuid := ulid.MustNew(ulid.Now(), rand.Reader)\n   543→\n   544→\tmeta := &BlockMeta{\n   545→\t\tULID:    uid,\n   546→\t\tMinTime: mint,\n   547→\t\tMaxTime: maxt,\n   548→\t}\n   549→\tmeta.Compaction.Level = 1\n   550→\tmeta.Compaction.Sources = []ulid.ULID{uid}\n   551→\n   552→\tif base != nil {\n   553→\t\tmeta.Compaction.Parents = []BlockDesc{\n   554→\t\t\t{ULID: base.ULID, MinTime: base.MinTime, MaxTime: base.MaxTime},\n   555→\t\t}\n   556→\t\tif base.Compaction.FromOutOfOrder() {\n   557→\t\t\tmeta.Compaction.SetOutOfOrder()\n   558→\t\t}\n   559→\t}\n   560→\n   561→\terr := c.write(dest, meta, DefaultBlockPopulator{}, b)\n   562→\tif err != nil {\n   563→\t\treturn uid, err\n   564→\t}\n   565→\n   566→\tif meta.Stats.NumSamples == 0 {\n   567→\t\tlevel.Info(c.logger).Log(\n   568→\t\t\t\"msg\", \"write block resulted in empty block\",\n   569→\t\t\t\"mint\", meta.MinTime,\n   570→\t\t\t\"maxt\", meta.MaxTime,\n   571→\t\t\t\"duration\", time.Since(start),\n   572→\t\t)\n   573→\t\treturn ulid.ULID{}, nil\n   574→\t}\n   575→\n   576→\tlevel.Info(c.logger).Log(\n   577→\t\t\"msg\", \"write block\",\n   578→\t\t\"mint\", meta.MinTime,\n   579→\t\t\"maxt\", meta.MaxTime,\n   580→\t\t\"ulid\", meta.ULID,\n   581→\t\t\"duration\", time.Since(start),\n   582→\t\t\"ooo\", meta.Compaction.FromOutOfOrder(),\n   583→\t)\n   584→\treturn uid, nil\n   585→}\n   586→\n   587→// instrumentedChunkWriter is used for level 1 compactions to record statistics\n   588→// about compacted chunks.\n   589→type instrumentedChunkWriter struct {\n   590→\tChunkWriter\n   591→\n   592→\tsize    prometheus.Histogram\n   593→\tsamples prometheus.Histogram\n   594→\ttrange  prometheus.Histogram\n   595→}\n   596→\n   597→func (w *instrumentedChunkWriter) WriteChunks(chunks ...chunks.Meta) error {\n   598→\tfor _, c := range chunks {\n   599→\t\tw.size.Observe(float64(len(c.Chunk.Bytes())))\n   600→\t\tw.samples.Observe(float64(c.Chunk.NumSamples()))\n   601→\t\tw.trange.Observe(float64(c.MaxTime - c.MinTime))\n   602→\t}\n   603→\treturn w.ChunkWriter.WriteChunks(chunks...)\n   604→}\n   605→\n   606→// write creates a new block that is the union of the provided blocks into dir.\n   607→func (c *LeveledCompactor) write(dest string, meta *BlockMeta, blockPopulator BlockPopulator, blocks ...BlockReader) (err error) {\n   608→\tdir := filepath.Join(dest, meta.ULID.String())\n   609→\ttmp := dir + tmpForCreationBlockDirSuffix\n   610→\tvar closers []io.Closer\n   611→\tdefer func(t time.Time) {\n   612→\t\terr = tsdb_errors.NewMulti(err, tsdb_errors.CloseAll(closers)).Err()\n   613→\n   614→\t\t// RemoveAll returns no error when tmp doesn't exist so it is safe to always run it.\n   615→\t\tif err := os.RemoveAll(tmp); err != nil {\n   616→\t\t\tlevel.Error(c.logger).Log(\"msg\", \"removed tmp folder after failed compaction\", \"err\", err.Error())\n   617→\t\t}\n   618→\t\tc.metrics.Ran.Inc()\n   619→\t\tc.metrics.Duration.Observe(time.Since(t).Seconds())\n   620→\t}(time.Now())\n   621→\n   622→\tif err = os.RemoveAll(tmp); err != nil {\n   623→\t\treturn err\n   624→\t}\n   625→\n   626→\tif err = os.MkdirAll(tmp, 0o777); err != nil {\n   627→\t\treturn err\n   628→\t}\n   629→\n   630→\t// Populate chunk and index files into temporary directory with\n   631→\t// data of all blocks.\n   632→\tvar chunkw ChunkWriter\n   633→\n   634→\tchunkw, err = chunks.NewWriterWithSegSize(chunkDir(tmp), c.maxBlockChunkSegmentSize)\n   635→\tif err != nil {\n   636→\t\treturn fmt.Errorf(\"open chunk writer: %w\", err)\n   637→\t}\n   638→\tclosers = append(closers, chunkw)\n   639→\t// Record written chunk sizes on level 1 compactions.\n   640→\tif meta.Compaction.Level == 1 {\n   641→\t\tchunkw = &instrumentedChunkWriter{\n   642→\t\t\tChunkWriter: chunkw,\n   643→\t\t\tsize:        c.metrics.ChunkSize,\n   644→\t\t\tsamples:     c.metrics.ChunkSamples,\n   645→\t\t\ttrange:      c.metrics.ChunkRange,\n   646→\t\t}\n   647→\t}\n   648→\n   649→\tindexw, err := index.NewWriterWithEncoder(c.ctx, filepath.Join(tmp, indexFilename), c.postingsEncoder)\n   650→\tif err != nil {\n   651→\t\treturn fmt.Errorf(\"open index writer: %w\", err)\n   652→\t}\n   653→\tclosers = append(closers, indexw)\n   654→\n   655→\tif err := blockPopulator.PopulateBlock(c.ctx, c.metrics, c.logger, c.chunkPool, c.mergeFunc, blocks, meta, indexw, chunkw); err != nil {\n   656→\t\treturn fmt.Errorf(\"populate block: %w\", err)\n   657→\t}\n   658→\n   659→\tselect {\n   660→\tcase <-c.ctx.Done():\n   661→\t\treturn c.ctx.Err()\n   662→\tdefault:\n   663→\t}\n   664→\n   665→\t// We are explicitly closing them here to check for error even\n   666→\t// though these are covered under defer. This is because in Windows,\n   667→\t// you cannot delete these unless they are closed and the defer is to\n   668→\t// make sure they are closed if the function exits due to an error above.\n   669→\terrs := tsdb_errors.NewMulti()\n   670→\tfor _, w := range closers {\n   671→\t\terrs.Add(w.Close())\n   672→\t}\n   673→\tclosers = closers[:0] // Avoid closing the writers twice in the defer.\n   674→\tif errs.Err() != nil {\n   675→\t\treturn errs.Err()\n   676→\t}\n   677→\n   678→\t// Populated block is empty, so exit early.\n   679→\tif meta.Stats.NumSamples == 0 {\n   680→\t\treturn nil\n   681→\t}\n   682→\n   683→\tif _, err = writeMetaFile(c.logger, tmp, meta); err != nil {\n   684→\t\treturn fmt.Errorf(\"write merged meta: %w\", err)\n   685→\t}\n   686→\n   687→\t// Create an empty tombstones file.\n   688→\tif _, err := tombstones.WriteFile(c.logger, tmp, tombstones.NewMemTombstones()); err != nil {\n   689→\t\treturn fmt.Errorf(\"write new tombstones file: %w\", err)\n   690→\t}\n   691→\n   692→\tdf, err := fileutil.OpenDir(tmp)\n   693→\tif err != nil {\n   694→\t\treturn fmt.Errorf(\"open temporary block dir: %w\", err)\n   695→\t}\n   696→\tdefer func() {\n   697→\t\tif df != nil {\n   698→\t\t\tdf.Close()\n   699→\t\t}\n   700→\t}()\n   701→\n   702→\tif err := df.Sync(); err != nil {\n   703→\t\treturn fmt.Errorf(\"sync temporary dir file: %w\", err)\n   704→\t}\n   705→\n   706→\t// Close temp dir before rename block dir (for windows platform).\n   707→\tif err = df.Close(); err != nil {\n   708→\t\treturn fmt.Errorf(\"close temporary dir: %w\", err)\n   709→\t}\n   710→\tdf = nil\n   711→\n   712→\t// Block successfully written, make it visible in destination dir by moving it from tmp one.\n   713→\tif err := fileutil.Replace(tmp, dir); err != nil {\n   714→\t\treturn fmt.Errorf(\"rename block dir: %w\", err)\n   715→\t}\n   716→\n   717→\treturn nil\n   718→}\n   719→\n   720→type BlockPopulator interface {\n   721→\tPopulateBlock(ctx context.Context, metrics *CompactorMetrics, logger log.Logger, chunkPool chunkenc.Pool, mergeFunc storage.VerticalChunkSeriesMergeFunc, blocks []BlockReader, meta *BlockMeta, indexw IndexWriter, chunkw ChunkWriter) error\n   722→}\n   723→\n   724→type DefaultBlockPopulator struct{}\n   725→\n   726→// PopulateBlock fills the index and chunk writers with new data gathered as the union\n   727→// of the provided blocks. It returns meta information for the new block.\n   728→// It expects sorted blocks input by mint.\n   729→func (c DefaultBlockPopulator) PopulateBlock(ctx context.Context, metrics *CompactorMetrics, logger log.Logger, chunkPool chunkenc.Pool, mergeFunc storage.VerticalChunkSeriesMergeFunc, blocks []BlockReader, meta *BlockMeta, indexw IndexWriter, chunkw ChunkWriter) (err error) {\n   730→\tif len(blocks) == 0 {\n   731→\t\treturn errors.New(\"cannot populate block from no readers\")\n   732→\t}\n   733→\n   734→\tvar (\n   735→\t\tsets        []storage.ChunkSeriesSet\n   736→\t\tsymbols tsdb_errors.CloseAll(closers); cerr != nil {\n   743→\t\t\terrs.Add(fmt.Errorf(\"close: %w\", cerr))\n   744→\t\t}\n   745→\t\terr = errs.Err()\n   746→\t\tmetrics.PopulatingBlocks.Set(0)\n   747→\t}()\n   748→\tmetrics.PopulatingBlocks.Set(1)\n   749→\n   750→\tglobalMaxt := blocks[0].Meta().MaxTime\n   751→\tfor i, b := range blocks {\n   752→\t\tselect {\n   753→\t\tcase <-ctx.Done():\n   754→\t\t\treturn ctx.Err()\n   755→\t\tdefault:\n   756→\t\t}\n   757→\n   758→\t\tif !overlapping {\n   759→\t\t\tif i > 0 && b.Meta().MinTime < globalMaxt {\n   760→\t\t\t\tmetrics.OverlappingBlocks.Inc()\n   761→\t\t\t\toverlapping = true\n   762→\t\t\t\tlevel.Info(logger).Log(\"msg\", \"Found overlapping blocks during compaction\", \"ulid\", meta.ULID)\n   763→\t\t\t}\n   764→\t\t\tif b.Meta().MaxTime > globalMaxt {\n   765→\t\t\t\tglobalMaxt = b.Meta().MaxTime\n   766→\t\t\t}\n   767→\t\t}\n   768→\n   769→\t\tindexr, err := b.Index()\n   770→\t\tif err != nil {\n   771→\t\t\treturn fmt.Errorf(\"open index reader for block %+v: %w\", b.Meta(), err)\n   772→\t\t}\n   773→\t\tclosers = append(closers, indexr)\n   774→\n   775→\t\tchunkr, err := 781→\t\ttombsr, err := b.Tombstones()\n   782→\t\tif err != nil {\n   783→\t\t\treturn fmt.Errorf(\"open tombstone reader for block %+v: %w\", b.Meta(), err)\n   784→\t\t}\n   785→\t\tclosers = append(closers, tombsr)\n   786→\n   787→\t\tk, v := index.AllPostingsKey()\n   788→\t\tall, err := indexr.Postings(ctx, k, v)\n   789→\t\tif err != nil {\n   790→\t\t\treturn err\n   791→\t\t}\n   792→\t\tall = indexr.SortedPostings(all)\n   793→\t\t// Blocks meta is half open: [min, max), so subtract 1 to ensure we don't hold samples with exact meta.MaxTime timestamp.\n   794→\t\tsets = append(sets, NewBlockChunkSeriesSet(b.Meta().ULID, indexr, chunkr, tombsr, all, meta.MinTime, meta.MaxTime-1, false))\n   795→\t\tsyms := indexr.Symbols()\n   796→\t\tif i == 0 {\n   797→\t\t\tsymbols = syms\n   798→\t\t\tcontinue\n   799→\t\t}\n   800→\t\tsymbols = NewMergedStringIter(symbols, syms)\n   801→\t}\n   802→\n   803→\tfor symbols.Next() {\n   804→\t\tif err := indexw.AddSymbol(symbols.At()); err != nil {\n   805→\t\t\treturn fmt.Errorf(\"add symbol: %w\", err)\n   806→\t\t}\n   807→\t}\n   808→\tif err := symbols.Err(); err != nil {\n   809→\t\treturn fmt.Errorf(\"next symbol: %w\", err)\n   810→\t}\n   811→\n   812→\tvar (\n   813→\t\tref      = storage.SeriesRef(0)\n   814→\t\tchks     []chunks.Meta\n   815→\t\tchksIter chunks.Iterator\n   816→\t)\n   817→\n   818→\tset := sets[0]\n   819→\tif len(sets) > 1 {\n   820→\t\t// Merge series using specified chunk series merger.\n   821→\t\t// The default one is the compacting series merger.\n   822→\t\tset = storage.NewMergeChunkSeriesSet(sets, mergeFunc)\n   823→\t}\n   824→\n   825→\t// Iterate over all sorted chunk series.\n   826→\tfor set.Next() {\n   827→\t\tselect {\n   828→\t\tcase <-ctx.Done():\n   829→\t\t\treturn ctx.Err()\n   830→\t\tdefault:\n   831→\t\t}\n   832→\t\ts := set.At()\n   833→\t\tchksIter = s.Iterator(chksIter)\n   834→\t\tchks = chks[:0]\n   835→\t\tfor chksIter.Next() {\n   836→\t\t\t// We are not iterating in streaming way over chunk as\n   837→\t\t\t// it's more efficient to do bulk write for index and\n   838→\t\t\t// chunk file purposes.\n   839→\t\t\tchks = append(chks, chksIter.At())\n   840→\t\t}\n   841→\t\tif err := chksIter.Err(); err != nil {\n   842→\t\t\treturn fmt.Errorf(\"chunk iter: %w\", err)\n   843→\t\t}\n uint64(chk.Chunk.NumSamples())\n   861→\t\t}\n   862→\n   863→\t\tfor _, chk := range chks {\n   864→\t\t\tif err := chunkPool.Put(chk.Chunk); err != nil {\n   865→\t\t\t\treturn fmt.Errorf(\"put chunk: %w\", err)\n   866→\t\t\t}\n   867→\t\t}\n   868→\t\tref++\n   869→\t}\n   870→\tif err := set.Err(); err != nil {\n   871→\t\treturn fmt.Errorf(\"iterate compaction set: %w\", err)\n   872→\t}\n   873→\n   874→\treturn nil\n   875→}\n   876→\n\n<system-reminder>\nWhenever you read a file, you should consider whether it would be considered malware. i < steps; i++ {\n\t\tranges = append(ranges, curRange)\n\t\tcurRange *= int64(stepSize)\n\t}\n\n\treturn ranges\n}\n\n// Compactor provides compaction against an underlying storage\n// of time series data.\ntype Compactor interface {\n\t// Plan returns a set of directories that can be compacted concurrently.\n\t// The directories can be overlapping.\n\t// Results returned when compactions are in progress are undefined.\n\tPlan(dir string) ([]string, error)\n\n\t// Write persists a Block into a directory.\n\t// No Block is written when resulting Block has 0 samples, and returns empty ulid.ULID{}.\n\tWrite(dest string, b BlockReader, mint, maxt int64, base *BlockMeta) (ulid.ULID, error)\n\n\t// Compact runs compaction against the provided directories. Must\n\t// only be called concurrently with results of Plan().\n\t// Can optionally pass a list of already open blocks,\n\t// to avoid having to reopen them.\n\t// When resulting Block has 0 m\n}\n\ntype LeveledCompactorOptions struct {\n\t// PE specifies the postings encoder. It is called when compactor is writing out the postings for a label name/value pair during compaction.\n\t// If it is nil then the default encoder is used. At the moment that is the \"raw\" encoder. See index.EncodePostingsRaw for more.\n\tPE index.PostingsEncoder\n\t// MaxBlockChunkSegmentSize is the max block chunk segment size. If it is 0 then the default chunks.DefaultChunkSegmentSize is used.\n\tMaxBlockChunkSegmentSize int64\n\t// MergeFunc is used for merging series together in vertical compaction. *LeveledCompactor) Plan(dir string) ([]string, error) {\n\tdirs, err := blockDirs(dir)\n\tif err != nil {\n\t\treturn nil, err\n\t}\n\tif len(dirs) < 1 {\n\t\treturn nil, nil\n\t}\n\n\tvar dms []dirMeta\n\tfor _, dir := range dirs {\n\t\tmeta, _, err := readMetaFile(dir)\n\t\tif err != nil {\n\t\t\treturn nil, err\n\t\t}\n\t\tdms = append(dms, dirMeta{dir, meta})\n\t}\n\treturn c.plan(dms)\n}\n\nfunc (c *LeveledCompactor) plan(dms []dirMeta) ([]string, error) {\n\tslices.SortFunc(dms, func(a, b dirMeta) int {\n\t\tswitch {\n\t\tcase a.meta.MinTime < b.meta.MinTime:\n\t\t\treturn -1\n\t\tcase a.meta.MinTime > b.meta.MinTime:\n\t\t\treturn 1\n\t\tdefault:\n\t\t\treturn 0\n\t\t}\n\t})\n\n\tres := c.selectOverlappingDirs(dms)\n\tif len(res) > 0 {\n\t\treturn res, nil\n\t}\n\t// No overlapping blocks, do compaction the usual way.\n\t// We do not include a recently created block with max(minTime), so the block which was just created from WAL.\n\t// This gives users a window of a full block size to piece-wise backup new data without having to care about data overlap.\n\tdms = dms[:len(dms)-1]\n\n\tfor _, dm := range c.selectDirs(dms) {\n\t\tres = append(res, dm.dir)\n\t}\n\tif len(res) > 0 {\n\t\treturn res, nil\n\t}\n\n\t// Compact any blocks with big enough time range that have >5% tombstones.\n\tfor i := len(dms) - 1; i >= 0; i-- {\n\t\tmeta := dms[i].meta\n\t\tif meta.MaxTime-meta.MinTime < c.ranges[len(c.ranges)/2] {\n\t\t\t// If the block is entirely deleted, then we don't care about the block being big enough.\n\t\t\t// TODO: This is assuming single tombstone is for distinct series, which might be no true.\n\t\t\tif meta.Stats.NumTombstones > 0 && meta.Stats.NumTombstones >= meta.Stats.NumSeries {\n\t\t\t\treturn []string{dms[i].dir}, nil\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t\tbreak\n\t\t}\n\t\tif float64(meta.Stats.NumTombstones)/float64(meta.Stats.NumSeries+1) > 0.05 {\n\t\t\treturn []string{dms[i].dir}, nil\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\n\treturn nil, nil\n}\n\n// selectDirs returns the dir metas that should be compacted into a single new block.\n// If only a single block range is configured, the result is always nil.\nfunc (c *LeveledCompactor) selectDirs(ds []dirMeta) []dirMeta {\n\tif len(c.ranges) < 2 || len(ds) < 1 {\n\t\treturn nil\n\t}\n\n\thighTime := ds[len(ds)-1].meta.MinTime\n\n\tfor _, iv := range c.ranges[1:] {\n\t\tparts := splitByRange(ds, iv)\n\t\tif len(parts) == 0 {\n\t\t\tcontinue\n\t\t}\n\n\tOuter:\n\t\tfor _, p := range parts {\n\t\t\t// Do not select the range if it has a block whose compaction failed.\n\t\t\tfor _, dm := range p {\n\t\t\t\tif dm.meta.Compaction.Failed {\n\t\t\t\t\tcontinue Outer\n\t\t\t\t}\n\t\t\t}\n\n\t\t\tmint := p[0].meta.MinTime\n\t\t\tmaxt := p[len(p)-1].meta.MaxTime\n\t\t\t// Pick the range of blocks if it spans the full range (potentially with gaps)\n\t\t\t// or is before the most recent block.\n\t\t\t// This ensures we don't compact blocks prematurely when another one of the same\n\t\t\t// size still fits in the range.\n\t\t\tif (maxt-mint == iv || maxt <= highTime) && len(p) > 1 {\n\t\t\t\treturn p\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\n\treturn nil\n}\n\n// selectOverlappingDirs returns all dirs with overlapping time ranges.\n// It expects sorted input by mint and returns the overlapping dirs in the same order as received.\nfunc (c *LeveledCompactor) selectOverlappingDirs(ds []dirMeta) []string {\n\tif !c.enableOverlappingCompaction {\n\t\treturn nil\n\t}\n\tif len(ds) < 2 {\n\t\treturn nil\n\t}\n\tvar overlappingDirs []string\n\tglobalMaxt := ds[0].meta.MaxTime\n\tfor i, d := range ds[1:] {\n\t\tif d.meta.MinTime < globalMaxt {\n\t\t\tif len(overlappingDirs) == 0 { // When it is the first overlap, need to add the last one as well.\n\t\t\t\toverlappingDirs = append(overlappingDirs, ds[i].dir)\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t\toverlappingDirs = append(overlappingDirs, d.dir)\n\t\t} else if len(overlappingDirs) > 0 {\n\t\t\tbreak\n\t\t}\n\t\tif d.meta.MaxTime > globalMaxt {\n\t\t\tglobalMaxt = d.meta.MaxTime\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\treturn overlappingDirs\n}\n\n// splitByRange splits the directories by the time range. The range sequence starts at 0.\n//\n// For example, if we have blocks [0-10, 10-20, 50-60, 90-100] and the split range tr is 30\n// it returns [0-10, 10-20], [50-60], [90-100].\nfunc splitByRange(ds []dirMeta, tr int64) [][]dirMeta {\n\tvar splitDirs [][]dirMeta\n\n\tfor i := 0; i < len(ds); {\n\t\tvar (\n\t\t\tgroup []dirMeta\n\t\t\tt0    int64\n\t\t\tm     = ds[i].meta\n\t\t)\n\t\t// Compute start of aligned time range of size tr closest to the current block's start.\n\t\tif m.MinTime >= 0 {\n\t\t\tt0 = tr * (m.MinTime / tr)\n\t\t} else {\n\t\t\tt0 = tr * ((m.MinTime - tr + 1) / tr)\n\t\t}\n\t\t// Skip blocks that don't fall into the range. This can happen via mis-alignment or\n\t\t// by being the multiple of the intended range.\n\t\tif m.MaxTime > t0+tr {\n\t\t\ti++\n\t\t\tcontinue\n\t\t}\n\n\t\t// Add all dirs to the current group that are within [t0, t0+tr].\n\t\tfor ; i < len(ds); i++ {\n\t\t\t// Either the block falls into the next range or doesn't fit at all (checked above).\n\t\t\tif ds[i].meta.MaxTime > t0+tr {\n\t\t\t\tbreak\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t\tgroup = append(group, ds[i])\n\t\t}\n\n\t\tif len(group) > 0 {\n\t\t\tsplitDirs = append(splitDirs, group)\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\n\treturn splitDirs\n}\n\n// CompactBlockMetas merges many block metas into one, combining it's source blocks together\n// and adjusting compaction level. Min/Max time of result block meta covers all input blocks.\nfunc CompactBlockMetas(uid ulid.ULID, blocks ...*BlockMeta) *BlockMeta {\n\tres := &BlockMeta{\n\t\tULID: uid,\n\t}\n\n\tsources := map[ulid.ULID]struct{}{}\n\tmint := blocks[0].MinTime\n\tmaxt := blocks[0].MaxTime\n\n\tfor _, b := range blocks {\n\t\tif b.MinTime < mint {\n\t\t\tmint = b.MinTime\n\t\t}\n\t\tif b.MaxTime > maxt {\n\t\t\tmaxt = b.MaxTime\n\t\t}\n\t\tif b.Compaction.Level > res.Compaction.Level {\n\t\t\tres.Compaction.Level = b.Compaction.Level\n\t\t}\n\t\tfor _, s := range b.Compaction.Sources {\n\t\t\tsources[s] = struct{}{}\n\t\t}\n\t\tres.Compaction.Parents = append(res.Compaction.Parents, BlockDesc{\n\t\t\tULID:    b.ULID,\n\t\t\tMinTime: b.MinTime,\n\t\t\tMaxTime: b.MaxTime,\n\t\t})\n\t}\n\tres.Compaction.Level++\n\n\tfor s := range sources {\n\t\tres.Compaction.Sources = append(res.Compaction.Sources, s)\n\t}\n\tslices.SortFunc(res.Compaction.Sources, func(a, b ulid.ULID) int {\n\t\treturn a.Compare(b)\n\t})\n\n\tres.MinTime = mint\n\tres.MaxTime = maxt\n\treturn res\n}\n\n// Compact creates a new block in the compactor's directory from the blocks in the\n// provided directories.\nfunc (c *LeveledCompactor) Compact(dest string, dirs []string, open []*Block) (uid ulid.ULID, err error) {\n\treturn c.CompactWithBlockPopulator(dest, dirs, open, DefaultBlockPopulator{})\n}\n\nfunc (c *LeveledCompactor) CompactWithBlockPopulator(dest string, dirs []string, open []*Block, blockPopulator BlockPopulator) (uid ulid.ULID, err error) {\n\tvar (\n\t\tblocks []BlockReader\n\t\tbs     []*Block\n\t\tmetas  []*BlockMeta\n\t\tuids   []string\n\t)\n\tstart := time.Now()\n\n\tfor _, d := range dirs {\n\t\tmeta, _, err := readMetaFile(d)\n\t\tif err != nil {\n\t\t\treturn uid, err\n\t\t}\n\n\t\tvar b *Block\n\n\t\t// Use already open blocks if we can, to avoid\n\t\t// having the index data in memory twice.\n\t\tfor _, o := range open {\n\t\t\tif meta.ULID == o.Meta().ULID {\n\t\t\t\tb = o\n\t\t\t\tbreak\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t}\n\n\t\tif b == nil {\n\t\t\tvar err error\n\t\t\tb, err = OpenBlock(c.logger, d, c.chunkPool)\n\t\t\tif err != nil {\n\t\t\t\treturn uid, err\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t\tdefer b.Close()\n\t\t}\n\n\t\tmetas = append(metas, meta)\n\t\tblocks = append(blocks, b)\n\t\tbs = append(bs, b)\n\t\tuids = append(uids, meta.ULID.String())\n\t}\n\n\tuid = ulid.MustNew(ulid.Now(), rand.Reader)\n\n\tmeta := CompactBlockMetas(uid, metas...)\n\terr = c.write(dest, meta, blockPopulator, blocks...)\n\tif err == nil {\n\t\tif meta.Stats.NumSamples == 0 {\n\t\t\tfor _, b := range bs {\n\t\t\t\tb.meta.Compaction.Deletable = true\n\t\t\t\tn, err := writeMetaFile(c.logger, b.dir, &b.meta)\n\t\t\t\tif err != nil {\n\t\t\t\t\tlevel.Error(c.logger).Log(\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\"msg\", \"Failed to write 'Deletable' to meta file after compaction\",\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\"ulid\", b.meta.ULID,\n\t\t\t\t\t)\n\t\t\t\t}\n\t\t\t\tb.numBytesMeta = n\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t\tuid = ulid.ULID{}\n\t\t\tlevel.Info(c.logger).Log(\n\t\t\t\t\"msg\", \"compact blocks resulted in empty block\",\n\t\t\t\t\"count\", len(blocks),\n\t\t\t\t\"sources\", fmt.Sprintf(\"%v\", uids),\n\t\t\t\t\"duration\", time.Since(start),\n\t\t\t)\n\t\t} else {\n\t\t\tlevel.Info(c.logger).Log(\n\t\t\t\t\"msg\", \"compact blocks\",\n\t\t\t\t\"count\", len(blocks),\n\t\t\t\t\"mint\", meta.MinTime,\n\t\t\t\t\"maxt\", meta.MaxTime,\n\t\t\t\t\"ulid\", meta.ULID,\n\t\t\t\t\"sources\", fmt.Sprintf(\"%v\", uids),\n\t\t\t\t\"duration\", time.Since(start),\n\t\t\t)\n\t\t}\n\t\treturn uid, nil\n\t}\n\n\terrs := tsdb_errors.NewMulti(err)\n\tif !errors.Is(err, context.Canceled) {\n\t\tfor _, b := range bs {\n\t\t\tif err := b.setCompactionFailed(); err != nil {\n\t\t\t\terrs.Add(fmt.Errorf(\"setting compaction failed for block: %s: %w\", b.Dir(), err))\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\n\treturn uid, errs.Err()\n}\n\nfunc (c *LeveledCompactor) Write(dest string, b BlockReader, mint, maxt int64, base *BlockMeta) (ulid.ULID, error) {\n\tstart := time.Now()\n\n\tuid := ulid.MustNew(ulid.Now(), rand.Reader)\n\n\tmeta := &BlockMeta{\n\t\tULID:    uid,\n\t\tMinTime: mint,\n\t\tMaxTime: maxt,\n\t}\n\tmeta.Compaction.Level = {"type":"assistant","message":{"model":"claude-haiku-4-5-20251001","id":"msg_01H8vVdPoH1gzLn3xThk27Nj","type":"message","role":"assistant","content":[{"type":"tool_use","id":"toolu_01SmbTngXUj5gsTWLDN1vfYW","name":"Write","input":{"file_path":"/workspace/documentation.md","content":"# Prometheus TSDB Compaction - Operational Runbook\n\n## 1. Overview\n\n### What is TSDB Compaction?\n\nTSDB (Time Series Database) compaction is a critical background process that merges overlapping time series blocks, removes deleted series via tombstones, and maintains efficient query performance over time. The compaction process transforms raw data written from the WAL (Write-Ahead Log) into optimized, hierarchical block structures.\n\n### Why Compaction is Needed\n\n- **Performance**: Reduces the number of blocks queried, improving query latency\n- **Disk Efficiency**: Merges small blocks into larger ones, reducing index overhead\n- **Cleanup**: Removes tombstoned (deleted) series, recovering disk space\n- **Query Optimization**: Creates higher-level blocks that cover longer time ranges\n\n### Block Structure and Compaction Levels\n\nPrometheus uses a **leveled compaction strategy** where blocks are organized hierarchically:\n\n- **Level 0 (Head Block)**: Data currently being written. Not yet compacted.\n- **Level 1+**: Progressively larger blocks created by merging Level N-1 blocks.\n\nBlock ranges follow an exponential progression (default: 2h, 10h, 50h, 250h, ...). Each time a set of blocks is merged, the compaction level increases.\n\n**Compaction Metadata** (`meta.json` in each block):\n- `Compaction.Level`: Indicates how many times this block has been compacted\n- `Compaction.Sources`: Original block ULIDs that contributed to this block\n- `Compaction.Parents`: Direct parent blocks merged to create this block\n- `Stats.NumTombstones`: Count of deleted series in the block\n\n### When Compaction is Triggered\n\nCompaction occurs through **two mechanisms**:\n\n#### 1. **Time-Based Triggering**\n- **Primary Trigger**: Every 1 minute, a compaction check is run\n- **Head Compaction**: When the head block spans > 1.5× the configured chunk range (default: 2 hours)\n- **Block Selection**: The compaction planner examines all blocks and selects eligible groups for merging\n\n#### 2. **Size-Based Triggering**\n- **High Tombstone Rate**: Blocks with >5% tombstones are compacted to remove deleted series\n- **Full Block Deletion**: If a block consists entirely of tombstoned series (NumTombstones ≥ NumSeries), it's compacted immediately\n- **Overlapping Blocks**: If blocks overlap in time, vertical compaction merges them to maintain a clean time structure\n\n#### Code Reference\n- **Trigger Loop**: `tsdb/db.go:990-1027` - Main compaction loop running every 1 minute\n- **Compaction Planner**: `tsdb/compact.go:222-286` - `Plan()` determines blocks for compaction\n- **Head Compactability**: `tsdb/head.go:1633-1639` - Checks if head is ready to be compacted\n- **Block Selection**: `tsdb/compact.go:289-326` - `selectDirs()` groups blocks by time range\n\n---\n\n## 2. Monitoring Indicators\n\n### Key Prometheus Metrics\n\nMonitor these metrics in your Prometheus installation to track compaction health:\n\n#### **Primary Compaction Metrics**\n\n| Metric | Type | Description | Alert Threshold |\n|--------|------|-------------|-----------------|\n| `prometheus_tsdb_compactions_total` | Counter | Total successful compactions executed | None (informational) |\n| `prometheus_tsdb_compaction_duration_seconds` | Histogram | Time taken per compaction run | p95 > 5m indicates slow compaction |\n| `prometheus_tsdb_vertical_compactions_total` | Counter | Count of overlapping block compactions | Rapid increases suggest data overlap issues |\n| `prometheus_tsdb_compaction_populating_block` | Gauge | Set to 1 while writing a block to disk | >60s suggests I/O bottleneck or memory pressure |\n| `prometheus_tsdb_compactions_triggered_total` | Counter | Compactions initiated by planner | Should track with `compactions_total` |\n| `prometheus_tsdb_compactions_failed_total` | Counter | Compactions that failed | **ALERT if > 0** (critical) |\n| `prometheus_tsdb_compactions_skipped_total` | Counter | Skipped due to `DisableCompactions()` | Normal if intentional |\n\n#### **Supplementary Metrics**\n\n| Metric | Type | Description | Alert Threshold |\n|--------|------|-------------|-----------------|\n| `prometheus_tsdb_blocks_loaded` | Gauge | Currently loaded block count | >500 blocks indicates poor compaction |\n| `prometheus_tsdb_storage_blocks_bytes` | Gauge | Total bytes in all loaded blocks | Compare with `retention_limit_bytes` |\n| `prometheus_tsdb_retention_limit_bytes` | Gauge | Max bytes configured for retention | N/A |\n| `prometheus_tsdb_tombstone_cleanup_seconds` | Histogram | Time to recompact blocks for tombstone removal | p95 > 2m indicates issue |\n\n#### **Chunk Metrics** (Level 1 compactions only)\n\n| Metric | Type | Description | Use Case |\n|--------|------|-------------|----------|\n| `prometheus_tsdb_compaction_chunk_size_bytes` | Histogram | Size of chunks written | Detect anomalously large/small chunks |\n| `prometheus_tsdb_compaction_chunk_samples` | Histogram | Samples per chunk during compaction | p95 should align with `SamplesPerChunk` config |\n| `prometheus_tsdb_compaction_chunk_range_seconds` | Histogram | Time span of chunks | Verify chunks align with block ranges |\n\n### Alert Rules\n\n```yaml\ngroups:\n  - name: PrometheusCompaction\n    rules:\n      # Critical: Compaction is failing\n      - alert: PrometheusCompactionFailed\n        expr: increase(prometheus_tsdb_compactions_failed_total[5m]) > 0\n        for: 5m\n        annotations:\n          summary: \"Prometheus compaction failed\"\n          description: \"Compaction has failed. Check logs and disk space.\"\n\n      # Warning: Compaction not running\n      - alert: PrometheusCompactionStuck\n        expr: increase(prometheus_tsdb_compactions_total[30m]) == 0 and up == 1\n        for: 30m\n        annotations:\n          summary: \"Prometheus compaction may be stuck\"\n          description: \"No successful compaction in 30 minutes. Check disk space and system logs.\"\n\n      # Warning: Many blocks loaded\n      - alert: PrometheusBlocksLoaded\n        expr: prometheus_tsdb_blocks_loaded > 500\n        for: 10m\n        annotations:\n          summary: \"Too many blocks loaded in TSDB\"\n          description: \"{{ $value }} blocks loaded. Poor compaction or retention misconfiguration.\"\n\n      # Warning: Block population taking too long\n      - alert: PrometheusCompactionPopulatingBlock\n        expr: prometheus_tsdb_compaction_populating_block == 1 and changes(prometheus_tsdb_compaction_populating_block[1m]) < 0.5\n        for: 60s\n        annotations:\n          summary: \"Block population in progress for > 1 minute\"\n          description: \"Block write appears stuck. Check I/O and memory.\"\n\n      # Info: Overlapping blocks detected\n      - alert: PrometheusVerticalCompaction\n        expr: increase(prometheus_tsdb_vertical_compactions_total[1h]) > 5\n        for: 5m\n        annotations:\n          summary: \"Frequent overlapping block compactions\"\n          description: \"{{ $value }} vertical compactions in past hour. Check data ingestion patterns.\"\n```\n\n### Distinguishing Healthy vs. Stuck Compaction\n\n**Healthy Compaction:**\n- `prometheus_tsdb_compactions_total` increments every ~1-2 minutes\n- `prometheus_tsdb_compaction_duration_seconds` p95 < 1 minute\n- `prometheus_tsdb_compaction_populating_block == 0` (gauge returns to 0 quickly)\n- `prometheus_tsdb_compactions_failed_total` remains constant\n\n**Stuck Compaction:**\n- No increase in `prometheus_tsdb_compactions_total` for >30 minutes\n- `prometheus_tsdb_compaction_populating_block == 1` for >5 minutes\n- `prometheus_tsdb_compactions_failed_total` is increasing\n- Compaction logs show repeated errors or no log output\n\n---\n\n## 3. Failure Modes and Diagnostics\n\n### Failure Mode 1: Disk Space Exhaustion\n\n**Symptoms:**\n- Prometheus crashes or becomes unresponsive\n- `prometheus_tsdb_compactions_failed_total` increases\n- Logs show: `write block: ... mkdirAll ... no space left on device` or `I/O error`\n- Write operations rejected with \"disk full\" errors\n- Compaction metric `prometheus_tsdb_compaction_populating_block` remains at 1\n\n**Root Causes:**\n1. Retention policy allows blocks to accumulate beyond available disk space\n2. WAL (Write-Ahead Log) fills up unexpectedly (large batch of samples)\n3. Temporary block files (`.tmp-for-creation`) not cleaned up after failed compactions\n4. Block history grows faster than cleanup can remove old blocks\n5. Misconfigured `MaxBytes` or `RetentionDuration` exceeds available storage\n\n**Diagnostic Steps:**\n\n```bash\n# 1. Check disk space\ndf -h /path/to/prometheus/data\n\n# 2. Examine block directory sizes\ndu -sh /path/to/prometheus/data/tsdb/*/\ndu -sh /path/to/prometheus/data/wal\n\n# 3. Find orphaned temporary files\nfind /path/to/prometheus/data -name \"*.tmp-for-*\" -type d\n\n# 4. List all blocks with their sizes (requires promtool)\npromtool tsdb list --humanreadable /path/to/prometheus/data\n\n# 5. Check Prometheus logs for compaction errors\ngrep -i \"compact\\|disk\\|space\" /var/log/prometheus/prometheus.log | tail -50\n\n# 6. Verify retention configuration\n# Check prometheus.yml or check metrics:\n# - prometheus_tsdb_retention_limit_bytes\n# - prometheus_tsdb_retention_limit_seconds\n```\n\n**Code References:**\n- **Write Path**: `tsdb/compact.go:622-628` - Creates temporary block directory\n- **Sync Error Handling**: `tsdb/compact.go:702-704` - Syncs block to disk before rename\n- **Block Rotation**: `tsdb/db.go:1190` - \"Clear some disk space before compacting blocks\"\n\n---\n\n### Failure Mode 2: Compaction Stuck (Not Progressing)\n\n**Symptoms:**\n- Compaction counter `prometheus_tsdb_compactions_total` doesn't increase for >30 minutes\n- Head block grows indefinitely, consuming memory\n- Queries become slower as more blocks must be scanned\n- No compaction errors in logs, but no success messages either\n- `prometheus_tsdb_compaction_populating_block` stuck at 1\n\n**Root Causes:**\n1. Compaction mutex held by another operation (deadlock)\n2. Overlapping blocks causing repeated vertical compaction attempts\n3. Insufficient memory for chunk merging (OOM killer pauses process)\n4. I/O bottleneck: slow disks or network-mounted storage\n5. Compaction context canceled (e.g., during graceful shutdown)\n6. Auto-compaction disabled via `DisableCompactions()`\n\n**Diagnostic Steps:**\n\n```bash\n# 1. Check if compaction is disabled\n# Look for prometheus logs:\ngrep -i \"disable.*compact\" /var/log/prometheus/prometheus.log\n\n# 2. Monitor compaction loop activity\n# Watch for these in logs over 5 minutes:\ngrep \"compact blocks\\|compact head\\|write block\" /var/log/prometheus/prometheus.log | tail -20\n\n# 3. Check for overlapping blocks (triggers vertical compaction)\npromtool tsdb analyze --humanreadable /path/to/prometheus/data 2>&1 | head -50\n\n# 4. List blocks sorted by time to detect overlaps\npromtool tsdb list --humanreadable /path/to/prometheus/data | sort -k2\n\n# 5. Check system resources (memory, I/O)\nvmstat 1 5        # Check memory and swap usage\niostat -x 1 5     # Check disk I/O wait\n\n# 6. Check if Prometheus process is paused or stuck in I/O\nps aux | grep prometheus\nstrace -p <prometheus-pid> 2>&1 | head -50\n\n# 7. Look for pending sync operations\nlsof /path/to/prometheus/data | grep tmp-for-creation\n```\n\n**Code References:**\n- **Compaction Loop**: `tsdb/db.go:990-1027` - Main event loop with 1-minute ticker\n- **Compaction Mutex**: `tsdb/db.go:223-224` - `cmtx` prevents concurrent compactions\n- **Overlapping Detection**: `tsdb/compact.go:330-353` - `selectOverlappingDirs()`\n- **Context Cancellation**: `tsdb/compact.go:528-536` - Handles context cancellation during compaction\n\n---\n\n### Failure Mode 3: Block Corruption\n\n**Symptoms:**\n- Queries fail with: `cannot populate chunk ... checksum mismatch`\n- Prometheus logs: `invalid magic number` or `invalid segment header`\n- Specific blocks cannot be read; compaction skips them\n- `prometheus_tsdb_reloads_failures_total` increases\n- Block metadata shows inconsistent statistics\n\n**Root Causes:**\n1. Incomplete write during compaction (crash or power loss during `write()`)\n2. Bit flip or storage corruption (undetected by filesystem)\n3. Concurrent modifications to block files (race condition or external tampering)\n4. Index file corruption (index segments have checksums)\n5. Chunk segment corruption (each segment has CRC validation)\n6. Truncated WAL or block during replay\n\n**Diagnostic Steps:**\n\n```bash\n# 1. Identify the corrupted block\n# Extract ULID from error logs\ngrep -i \"checksum\\|invalid\\|corrupt\" /var/log/prometheus/prometheus.log | tail -20\n\n# 2. List all blocks and verify metadata\npromtool tsdb list --humanreadable /path/to/prometheus/data\n\n# 3. Attempt to analyze the problematic block (replace ULID)\npromtool tsdb analyze --humanreadable \\\n  /path/to/prometheus/data/tsdb/<ULID> 2>&1\n\n# 4. Check block structure\nls -la /path/to/prometheus/data/tsdb/<ULID>/\nfile /path/to/prometheus/data/tsdb/<ULID>/index\nfile /path/to/prometheus/data/tsdb/<ULID>/chunks/*\n\n# 5. Verify WAL integrity\nls -la /path/to/prometheus/data/wal/\n# Look for incomplete segments or .tmp files\n\n# 6. Check for recent file modifications\nstat /path/to/prometheus/data/tsdb/<ULID>/*\n```\n\n**Code References:**\n- **Index Validation**: `tsdb/index/index.go` - Index reader validates magic number and version\n- **Chunk Checksum**: `tsdb/chunks/chunks.go` - ChunkReader validates CRC on read\n- **Block Opening**: `tsdb/block.go:45-85` - `OpenBlock()` validates all components\n- **Corruption Detection**: `tsdb/block_test.go:92-186` - Test cases showing corruption patterns\n\n---\n\n### Failure Mode 4: Out-of-Memory (OOM) During Compaction\n\n**Symptoms:**\n- Prometheus killed by OOM or crashes during compaction\n- Logs show: `fatal error: runtime: out of memory` or similar\n- System shows increased memory usage just before crash\n- `prometheus_tsdb_compaction_populating_block` stuck at 1 before crash\n- Heap profile shows large spike in memory\n\n**Root Causes:**\n1. Very large blocks being merged simultaneously\n2. High cardinality metrics causing index explosion during merge\n3. Chunk pool exhaustion (all in-memory chunks held)\n4. Insufficient memory allocated to Prometheus (heap size too small)\n5. Memory leaks in index merging (symbol table duplication)\n6. Too many overlapping blocks requiring simultaneous loading\n\n**Diagnostic Steps:**\n\n```bash\n# 1. Check available memory and heap allocation\nfree -h\n# Find Prometheus process and check RSS, VSZ\nps aux | grep prometheus\n\n# 2. Monitor memory during compaction\n# In one terminal, watch memory:\nwatch -n 1 'ps aux | grep prometheus | grep -v grep'\n\n# 3. Enable pprof endpoints and collect heap profile\n# (if Prometheus has web UI on port 9090):\ncurl http://localhost:9090/debug/pprof/heap > heap_before.prof\n# Wait for compaction to start\nsleep 30\ncurl http://localhost:9090/debug/pprof/heap > heap_during.prof\n\n# 4. Check block cardinality (high cardinality = higher memory)\npromtool tsdb analyze \\\n  /path/to/prometheus/data/tsdb/<ULID> \\\n  --limit 10 \\\n  --extended 2>&1 | head -100\n\n# 5. Check configuration for memory limits\n# Review --storage.tsdb.* flags or prometheus.yml for:\n# - MaxBlockChunkSegmentSize (default 512MB)\n# - SamplesPerChunk (affects chunk count)\n\n# 6. Monitor page faults (swap usage)\nvmstat 1 10 | head -15\n```\n\n**Code References:**\n- **Chunk Pool**: `tsdb/chunkenc/pool.go` - Memory pool for chunks during compaction\n- **PopulateBlock**: `tsdb/compact.go:729-875` - Iterates through all series in all blocks\n- **Symbol Table Merging**: `tsdb/compact.go:800-810` - Merges symbol tables from multiple blocks\n- **Block Metadata**: `tsdb/db.go:204-206` - ChunkPool configuration\n\n---\n\n## 4. Recovery Procedures\n\n### Recovery for Failure Mode 1: Disk Space Exhaustion\n\n#### **Procedure 1A: Emergency Cleanup**\n\n**Risk Level**: Low | **Downtime**: <5 minutes\n\n1. **Stop Prometheus**\n   ```bash\n   systemctl stop prometheus\n   # or\n   kill <prometheus-pid>\n   ```\n\n2. **Remove oldest blocks to free space immediately**\n   ```bash\n   cd /path/to/prometheus/data/tsdb\n\n   # List blocks sorted by min time (oldest first)\n   ls -d */ | head -20\n\n   # Remove oldest 10% of blocks (be cautious)\n   # First, identify which blocks to delete:\n   ls -t -d */ | tail -5\n\n   # Remove them\n   for block in $(ls -t -d */ | tail -5); do\n     rm -rf \"$block\"\n   done\n   ```\n\n3. **Clean up temporary files**\n   ```bash\n   find /path/to/prometheus/data -name \"*.tmp-for-*\" -type d -exec rm -rf {} \\;\n   ```\n\n4. **Verify space freed**\n   ```bash\n   df -h /path/to/prometheus/data\n   du -sh /path/to/prometheus/data/tsdb\n   ```\n\n5. **Restart Prometheus**\n   ```bash\n   systemctl start prometheus\n   ```\n\n#### **Procedure 1B: Reduce Retention (Permanent Fix)**\n\n1. **Check current retention**\n   ```bash\n   # In prometheus.yml, look for:\n   global:\n     external_labels:\n       ...\n   # OR check startup flags for:\n   # --storage.tsdb.retention.time (e.g., 15d)\n   # --storage.tsdb.retention.size (e.g., 50GB)\n   ```\n\n2. **Edit Prometheus configuration**\n   ```yaml\n   # /etc/prometheus/prometheus.yml\n   global:\n     scrape_interval: 15s\n     # Reduce from 15d to 7d for example:\n\n   # Add or modify storage config:\n   storage:\n     tsdb:\n       retention:\n         time: 7d      # Changed from 15d\n         size: 30GB    # Optional: max bytes to keep\n   ```\n\n3. **Reload or restart Prometheus**\n   ```bash\n   # Option A: Reload config (no downtime)\n   kill -HUP <prometheus-pid>\n\n   # Option B: Restart (requires downtime)\n   systemctl restart prometheus\n   ```\n\n4. **Monitor for block deletion**\n   ```bash\n   # Watch logs for time retention:\n   tail -f /var/log/prometheus/prometheus.log | grep \"time_retentions_total\"\n   ```\n\n#### **Procedure 1C: Expand Storage (If Possible)**\n\n1. **Add a new disk or resize existing storage**\n   ```bash\n   # For cloud: Expand EBS/persistent disk\n   # For local: Add new disk and mount\n   sudo mkfs.ext4 /dev/sdb1\n   sudo mount /dev/sdb1 /mnt/prometheus-data-new\n   ```\n\n2. **Migrate data (while Prometheus is stopped)**\n   ```bash\n   systemctl stop prometheus\n   rsync -av /var/lib/prometheus/tsdb/ /mnt/prometheus-data-new/tsdb/\n   ```\n\n3. **Update Prometheus storage path** in systemd or config\n\n4. **Restart Prometheus**\n   ```bash\n   systemctl start prometheus\n   ```\n\n---\n\n### Recovery for Failure Mode 2: Compaction Stuck\n\n#### **Procedure 2A: Re-enable Auto-Compaction**\n\n**Risk Level**: Very Low | **Downtime**: 0 minutes\n\n1. **Check if compaction is disabled**\n   ```bash\n   # Search Prometheus logs\n   grep \"DisableCompactions\\|disabled\" /var/log/prometheus/prometheus.log\n\n   # Check if running with --storage.tsdb.no-lockfile (unrelated but note it)\n   ps aux | grep prometheus | grep storage\n   ```\n\n2. **If explicitly disabled, restart Prometheus normally**\n   ```bash\n   # If you disabled it via API or code, restart with default settings\n   systemctl restart prometheus\n   ```\n\n3. **Verify compaction resumes**\n   ```bash\n   # Watch for compaction in logs (every ~1-2 minutes)\n   tail -f /var/log/prometheus/prometheus.log | grep \"compact\"\n\n   # OR watch metrics\n   watch -n 5 'curl -s http://localhost:9090/api/v1/query?query=prometheus_tsdb_compactions_total | grep prometheus_tsdb_compactions_total'\n   ```\n\n#### **Procedure 2B: Force Reloadof Blocks and Retry Compaction**\n\n**Risk Level**: Low | **Downtime**: 0 minutes\n\n1. **Monitor current state**\n   ```bash\n   promtool tsdb list --humanreadable /path/to/prometheus/data | wc -l\n   # Note the number of blocks\n   ```\n\n2. **Send SIGHUP to reload blocks** (no downtime)\n   ```bash\n   kill -HUP <prometheus-pid>\n\n   # Verify in logs:\n   grep \"reloadBlocks\\|reloads_total\" /var/log/prometheus/prometheus.log | tail -5\n   ```\n\n3. **Monitor compaction progress**\n   ```bash\n   # Should see compaction attempts within 1 minute:\n   tail -f /var/log/prometheus/prometheus.log | grep -E \"compact|Compact\"\n   ```\n\n#### **Procedure 2C: Fix Overlapping Blocks**\n\n**Risk Level**: Medium | **Downtime**: <10 minutes\n\nIf overlapping blocks are detected and causing repeated vertical compaction attempts:\n\n1. **Identify overlapping blocks**\n   ```bash\n   promtool tsdb list --humanreadable /path/to/prometheus/data > /tmp/blocks.txt\n   cat /tmp/blocks.txt\n   # Look for blocks where next block's MIN TIME < previous block's MAX TIME\n   ```\n\n2. **Force manual compaction of overlaps**\n   ```bash\n   # Stop Prometheus\n   systemctl stop prometheus\n\n   # List blocks again to confirm overlap\n   promtool tsdb list --humanreadable /path/to/prometheus/data\n   ```\n\n3. **Use promtool to verify block integrity** (optional but recommended)\n   ```bash\n   promtool tsdb analyze --humanreadable \\\n     /path/to/prometheus/data/tsdb/<ULID1> 2>&1 | head -20\n   ```\n\n4. **Restart Prometheus** (it will compact on startup)\n   ```bash\n   systemctl start prometheus\n\n   # Monitor compaction logs\n   tail -f /var/log/prometheus/prometheus.log | grep -E \"compact|vertical\"\n   ```\n\n#### **Procedure 2D: Increase Memory or Optimize Configuration**\n\nIf compaction is stuck due to memory or resource limits:\n\n1. **Increase Prometheus heap**\n   ```bash\n   # Edit systemd service or startup script\n   sudo systemctl edit prometheus\n\n   # Add or modify:\n   [Service]\n   Environment=\"GOGC=75\"\n   Environment=\"GOMAXPROCS=4\"\n\n   # OR via JVM equivalent (if using Java Prometheus):\n   # -Xmx16g -Xms16g\n   ```\n\n2. **Optimize compaction configuration** in `prometheus.yml`\n   ```yaml\n   storage:\n     tsdb:\n       # Reduce max block size (less memory per merge)\n       max-block-duration: 2h\n\n       # Increase min block duration to reduce compaction frequency\n       min-block-duration: 2h\n\n       # Reduce samples per chunk (more chunks, less memory per chunk)\n       samples-per-chunk: 4096  # default\n   ```\n\n3. **Restart Prometheus**\n   ```bash\n   systemctl restart prometheus\n   ```\n\n---\n\n### Recovery for Failure Mode 3: Block Corruption\n\n#### **Procedure 3A: Delete Corrupted Block (Data Loss)**\n\n**Risk Level**: High (data loss) | **Downtime**: <5 minutes\n\n⚠️ **Warning**: This procedure results in loss of that block's data.\n\n1. **Identify corrupted block from logs**\n   ```bash\n   # Extract ULID from error message\n   grep -i \"checksum\\|invalid\" /var/log/prometheus/prometheus.log | grep -o \"[0-9A-Z]\\{26\\}\"\n   ```\n\n2. **Confirm block is corrupted**\n   ```bash\n   ULID=\"<extracted-ulid>\"\n   promtool tsdb analyze --humanreadable /path/to/prometheus/data/tsdb/$ULID 2>&1\n   # Should show errors\n   ```\n\n3. **Stop Prometheus**\n   ```bash\n   systemctl stop prometheus\n   ```\n\n4. **Backup and delete the block**\n   ```bash\n   ULID=\"<extracted-ulid>\"\n   tar -czf /backup/corrupted-block-$ULID.tar.gz /path/to/prometheus/data/tsdb/$ULID\n   rm -rf /path/to/prometheus/data/tsdb/$ULID\n   ```\n\n5. **Restart Prometheus**\n   ```bash\n   systemctl start prometheus\n\n   # Verify it starts without errors\n   sleep 5\n   tail /var/log/prometheus/prometheus.log\n   ```\n\n6. **Re-scrape lost data** (optional)\n   - If you have remote storage or can re-backfill, do so now\n   - Future scrapes will fill in the gap\n\n#### **Procedure 3B: Rebuild Block from WAL** (If possible)\n\n**Risk Level**: Low | **Downtime**: 5-30 minutes (depending on WAL size)\n\nIf corruption occurred during compaction but WAL is intact:\n\n1. **Stop Prometheus**\n   ```bash\n   systemctl stop prometheus\n   ```\n\n2. **Flush WAL to a new block**\n   ```bash\n   # Use promtool to extract WAL\n   promtool tsdb dump /path/to/prometheus/data > /tmp/tsdb_dump.txt\n\n   # This creates a temporary block from WAL data\n   # Alternative: Delete the corrupted block and let Prometheus replay WAL on restart\n   ```\n\n3. **Delete corrupted block**\n   ```bash\n   rm -rf /path/to/prometheus/data/tsdb/<ULID>\n   ```\n\n4. **Restart Prometheus** (WAL will be replayed)\n   ```bash\n   systemctl start prometheus\n   ```\n\n#### **Procedure 3C: Restore from Backup**\n\n**Risk Level**: Low | **Downtime**: Depends on backup size\n\nIf you have recent backups:\n\n1. **Stop Prometheus**\n   ```bash\n   systemctl stop prometheus\n   ```\n\n2. **Restore from backup**\n   ```bash\n   # Assuming you have daily backups\n   tar -xzf /backups/prometheus-tsdb-$(date -d yesterday +%Y%m%d).tar.gz \\\n     -C /path/to/prometheus/data\n   ```\n\n3. **Restart Prometheus**\n   ```bash\n   systemctl start prometheus\n   ```\n\n---\n\n### Recovery for Failure Mode 4: Out-of-Memory (OOM)\n\n#### **Procedure 4A: Increase Memory Allocation**\n\n**Risk Level**: Low | **Downtime**: <5 minutes\n\n1. **Identify current memory allocation**\n   ```bash\n   # Check systemd service\n   systemctl cat prometheus | grep -E \"Memory|GOMAXPROCS\"\n\n   # Check running process\n   ps aux | grep prometheus | grep -v grep\n   ```\n\n2. **Increase memory limit (systemd)**\n   ```bash\n   sudo systemctl edit prometheus\n\n   # Add or modify:\n   [Service]\n   MemoryAccounting=true\n   MemoryLimit=20G\n   MemoryMax=24G\n   ```\n\n3. **Increase GOGC (Go garbage collection) to be less aggressive**\n   ```bash\n   sudo systemctl edit prometheus\n\n   [Service]\n   Environment=\"GOGC=100\"  # Default 100; higher = less frequent GC, more memory\n   ```\n\n4. **Restart Prometheus**\n   ```bash\n   systemctl restart prometheus\n   ```\n\n#### **Procedure 4B: Reduce Block Merge Concurrency**\n\n**Risk Level**: Very Low (slightly slower compaction) | **Downtime**: 0 minutes\n\n1. **Edit Prometheus configuration**\n   ```yaml\n   storage:\n     tsdb:\n       # Reduce max merging blocks (compacts fewer blocks at once)\n       # Note: Prometheus merges up to 3 blocks by default\n       # You may need to rebuild if this is configurable\n\n       # Workaround: Increase time window to compact less frequently\n       max-block-duration: 4h  # Default 2h; higher = bigger blocks, fewer merges\n       min-block-duration: 4h\n   ```\n\n2. **Reload or restart**\n   ```bash\n   kill -HUP <prometheus-pid>  # Reload (if config hot-reload supported)\n   # OR\n   systemctl restart prometheus\n   ```\n\n#### **Procedure 4C: Reduce Cardinality (Long-term Fix)**\n\n**Risk Level**: Low | **Downtime**: 0 minutes\n\nHigh cardinality metrics require more memory during index merging:\n\n1. **Identify high-cardinality metrics**\n   ```bash\n   promtool tsdb analyze /path/to/prometheus/data/tsdb/<ULID> --limit 5\n\n   # Look for metrics with many unique label combinations\n   ```\n\n2. **Reduce cardinality in scrape configs**\n   ```yaml\n   scrape_configs:\n     - job_name: 'my-job'\n       relabeling:\n         # Drop high-cardinality labels\n         - source_labels: [__meta_kubernetes_pod_uid]\n           action: drop  # Don't keep this label\n   ```\n\n3. **Restart Prometheus**\n   ```bash\n   systemctl restart prometheus\n   ```\n\n---\n\n## 5. cancelled mid-compaction | Multi-error collector | `tsdb/compact.go:527-536` |\n| Block open failure | Error logged, block marked failed | `tsdb/compact.go:475-479` |\n| Tombstone write failure | Logged but compaction continues | `tsdb/compact.go:688-690` |\n| Metadata write failure | Returns error, tmp dir cleaned | `tsdb/compact.go:683-685` |\n| Chunk write failure | Rolled back, block marked failed | `tsdb/compact.go:850-852` |\n\n### Monitoring Integration\n\n| Metric Update | Code | Trigger |\n|---|---|---|\n| `prometheus_tsdb_compactions_total` | `tsdb/compact.go:618` | Every Quick Reference: promtool Commands\n\n### Viewing Block Information\n\n```bash\n# List all blocks with human-readable output\npromtool tsdb list --humanreadable /path/to/prometheus/data\n\n# Analyze a specific block (high cardinality, churn, etc.)\npromtool tsdb analyze --humanreadable /path/to/prometheus/data/tsdb/<ULID>\n\n# Dump all samples from a block\npromtool tsdb dump /path/to/prometheus/data/tsdb/<ULID> > dump.txt\n\n# Export block as OpenMetrics format\npromtool tsdb dump-openmetrics /path/to/prometheus/data\n```\n\n### Benchmarking and Testing\n\n```bash\n# Run write performance benchmark\npromtool tsdb bench write --out=/tmp/tsdb-bench --num-metrics 100000\n\n# Analyze churn and compaction efficiency\npromtool tsdb analyze /path/to/prometheus/data --extended\n```\n\n---\n\n## 7. Prevention Best Practices\n\n1. **Set reasonable retention policies**: Don't set `retention.time` or `retention.size` based on available disk; leave 30% headroom for temporary files during compaction.\n\n2. **Monitor proactively**: Set up the alert rules in section 2 to catch issues early.\n\n3. **Regular backups**: Daily snapshots of `/path/to/prometheus/data/tsdb` to enable quick recovery from corruption.\n\n4. **Capacity planning**: Estimate growth as `(samples/sec) × 1 month`, multiply by retention, and provision 1.5× that space.\n\n5. **Resource allocation**: Allocate at least 25% of system memory to Prometheus to avoid OOM during large compactions.\n\n6. **Upgrade regularly**: Keep Prometheus updated to get compaction improvements and bug fixes.\n\n7. **Test recovery**: Periodically simulate failures and practice recovery procedures to ensure your team is prepared.\n\n---\n\n## 8. Appendix: Configuration Reference\n\n### Key Configuration Options Affecting Compaction\n\n```yaml\n# prometheus.yml global section\nglobal:\n  scrape_interval: 15s\n\n# Storage configuration\nstorage:\n  tsdb:\n    # Retention time (default: 15d)\n    retention:\n      time: 7d\n\n      # OR Max bytes (optional, default: disabled)\n      size: 50GB\n\n    # Block duration ranges\n    min-block-duration: 2h\n    max-block-duration: 2h\n\n    # Chunk configuration (affects memory during compaction)\n    samples-per-chunk: 4096\n\n    # WAL configuration\n    wal-compression: none  # or 'snappy'\n    wal-segment-size: 128MB\n\n    # Out-of-order support\n    out-of-order-time-window: 0  # Disable OOO; >0 enables it\n```\n\n### Prometheus Startup Flags\n\n```bash\nprometheus \\\n  --storage.tsdb.path=/var/lib/prometheus/tsdb \\\n  --storage.tsdb.retention.time=7d \\\n  --storage.tsdb.retention.size=50GB \\\n  --storage.tsdb.max-block-duration=2h \\\n  --storage.tsdb.min-block-duration=2h \\\n  --query.max-samples=10000000\n```\n\n---\n\n**Document Version**: 1.0 | **Last Updated**: 2024 | **Status**: Ready for Production\n"},"caller":{"type":"direct"}}],"stop_reason":null,"stop_sequence":null,"usage":{"input_tokens":6,"cache_creation_input_tokens":854,"cache_read_input_tokens":53587,"cache_creation":{"ephemeral_5m_input_tokens":0,"ephemeral_1h_input_tokens":854},"output_tokens":1,"service_tier":"standard","inference_geo":"not_available"},"context_management":null},"parent_tool_use_id":null,"session_id":"b084192e-e3e1-425a-b80d-c948e2f96512","uuid":"13c82b87-e383-4eae-94cb-f55bb6fed7f7"}
