Overview\n\n### What is TSDB Compaction?\n\nTSDB (Time Series Database) compaction is a critical background process that merges overlapping time series blocks, removes deleted series via tombstones, and maintains efficient query performance over time. The compaction process transforms raw data written from the WAL (Write-Ahead Log) into optimized, hierarchical block structures.\n\n### Why Compaction is Needed\n\n- **Performance**: Reduces the number of blocks queried, improving query latency\n- **Disk Efficiency**: Merges small blocks into larger ones, reducing index overhead\n- **Cleanup**: Removes tombstoned (deleted) series, recovering disk space\n- **Query Optimization**: Creates higher-level blocks that cover longer time ranges\n\n### Block Structure and Compaction Levels\n\nPrometheus uses a **leveled compaction strategy** where blocks are organized hierarchically:\n\n- **Level 0 (Head Block)**: Data currently being written. Not yet compacted.\n- **Level 1+**: Progressively larger blocks created by merging Level N-1 blocks.\n\nBlock ranges follow an exponential progression (default: 2h, 10h, 50h, 250h, ...). Each time a set of blocks is merged, the compaction level increases.\n\n**Compaction Metadata** (`meta.json` in each block):\n- `Compaction.Level`: Indicates how many times this block has been compacted\n- `Compaction.Sources`: Original block ULIDs that contributed to this block\n- `Compaction.Parents`: Direct parent blocks merged to create this block\n- `Stats.NumTombstones`: Count of deleted series in the block\n\n### When Compaction is Triggered\n\nCompaction occurs through **two mechanisms**:\n\n#### 1. **Time-Based Triggering**\n- **Primary Trigger**: Every 1 minute, a compaction check is run\n- **Head Compaction**: When the head block spans > 1.5× the configured chunk range (default: 2 hours)\n- **Block Selection**: The compaction planner examines all blocks and selects eligible groups for merging\n\n#### 2. **Size-Based Triggering**\n- **High Tombstone Rate**: Blocks with >5% tombstones are compacted to remove deleted series\n- **Full Block Deletion**: If a block consists entirely of tombstoned series (NumTombstones ≥ NumSeries), it's compacted immediately\n- **Overlapping Blocks**: If blocks overlap in time, vertical compaction merges them to maintain a clean time structure\n\n#### Code Reference\n- **Trigger Loop**: `tsdb/db.go:990-1027` - Main compaction loop running every 1 minute\n- **Compaction Planner**: `tsdb/compact.go:222-286` - `Plan()` determines blocks for compaction\n- **Head Compactability**: `tsdb/head.go:1633-1639` - Checks if head is ready to be compacted\n- **Block Selection**: `tsdb/compact.go:289-326` - `selectDirs()` groups blocks by time range\n\n---\n\n## 2. Monitoring Indicators\n\n### Key Prometheus Metrics\n\nMonitor these metrics in your Prometheus installation to track compaction health:\n\n#### **Primary Compaction Metrics**\n\n| Metric | Type | Description | Alert Threshold |\n|--------|------|-------------|-----------------|\n| `prometheus_tsdb_compactions_total` | Counter | Total successful compactions executed | None (informational) |\n| `prometheus_tsdb_compaction_duration_seconds` | Histogram | Time taken per compaction run | p95 > 5m indicates slow compaction |\n| `prometheus_tsdb_vertical_compactions_total` | Counter | Count of overlapping block compactions | Rapid increases suggest data overlap issues |\n| `prometheus_tsdb_compaction_populating_block` | Gauge | Set to 1 while writing a block to disk | >60s suggests I/O bottleneck or memory pressure |\n| `prometheus_tsdb_compactions_triggered_total` | Counter | Compactions initiated by planner | Should track with `compactions_total` |\n| `prometheus_tsdb_compactions_failed_total` | Counter | Compactions that failed | **ALERT if > 0** (critical) |\n| `prometheus_tsdb_compactions_skipped_total` | Counter | Skipped due to `DisableCompactions()` | Normal if intentional |\n\n#### **Supplementary Metrics**\n\n| Metric | Type | Description | Alert Threshold |\n|--------|------|-------------|-----------------|\n| `prometheus_tsdb_blocks_loaded` | Gauge | Currently loaded block count | >500 blocks indicates poor compaction |\n| `prometheus_tsdb_storage_blocks_bytes` | Gauge | Total bytes in all loaded blocks | Compare with `retention_limit_bytes` |\n| `prometheus_tsdb_retention_limit_bytes` | Gauge | Max bytes configured for retention | N/A |\n| `prometheus_tsdb_tombstone_cleanup_seconds` | Histogram | Time to recompact blocks for tombstone removal | p95 > 2m indicates issue |\n\n#### **Chunk Metrics** (Level 1 compactions only)\n\n| Metric | Type | Description | Use Case |\n|--------|------|-------------|----------|\n| `prometheus_tsdb_compaction_chunk_size_bytes` | Histogram | Size of chunks written | Detect anomalously large/small chunks |\n| `prometheus_tsdb_compaction_chunk_samples` | Histogram | Samples per chunk during compaction | p95 should align with `SamplesPerChunk` config |\n| `prometheus_tsdb_compaction_chunk_range_seconds` | Histogram | Time span of chunks | Verify chunks align with block ranges |\n\n### Alert Rules\n\n```yaml\ngroups:\n  - name: PrometheusCompaction\n    rules:\n      # Critical: Compaction is failing\n      - alert: PrometheusCompactionFailed\n        expr: increase(prometheus_tsdb_compactions_failed_total[5m]) > 0\n        for: 5m\n        annotations:\n          summary: \"Prometheus compaction failed\"\n          description: \"Compaction has failed. Check logs and disk space.\"\n\n      # Warning: Compaction not running\n      - alert: PrometheusCompactionStuck\n        expr: increase(prometheus_tsdb_compactions_total[30m]) == 0 and up == 1\n        for: 30m\n        annotations:\n          summary: \"Prometheus compaction may be stuck\"\n          description: \"No successful compaction in 30 minutes. Check disk space and system logs.\"\n\n      # Warning: Many blocks loaded\n      - alert: PrometheusBlocksLoaded\n        expr: prometheus_tsdb_blocks_loaded > 500\n        for: 10m\n        annotations:\n          summary: \"Too many blocks loaded in TSDB\"\n          description: \"{{ $value }} blocks loaded. Poor compaction or retention misconfiguration.\"\n\n      # Warning: Block population taking too long\n      - alert: PrometheusCompactionPopulatingBlock\n        expr: prometheus_tsdb_compaction_populating_block == 1 and changes(prometheus_tsdb_compaction_populating_block[1m]) < 0.5\n        for: 60s\n        annotations:\n          summary: \"Block population in progress for > 1 minute\"\n          description: \"Block write appears stuck. Check I/O and memory.\"\n\n      # Info: Overlapping blocks detected\n      - alert: PrometheusVerticalCompaction\n        expr: increase(prometheus_tsdb_vertical_compactions_total[1h]) > 5\n        for: 5m\n        annotations:\n          summary: \"Frequent overlapping block compactions\"\n          description: \"{{ $value }} vertical compactions in past hour. Check data ingestion patterns.\"\n```\n\n### Distinguishing Healthy vs. Stuck Compaction\n\n**Healthy Compaction:**\n- `prometheus_tsdb_compactions_total` increments every ~1-2 minutes\n- `prometheus_tsdb_compaction_duration_seconds` p95 < 1 minute\n- `prometheus_tsdb_compaction_populating_block == 0` (gauge returns to 0 quickly)\n- `prometheus_tsdb_compactions_failed_total` remains constant\n\n**Stuck Compaction:**\n- No increase in `prometheus_tsdb_compactions_total` for >30 minutes\n- `prometheus_tsdb_compaction_populating_block == 1` for >5 minutes\n- `prometheus_tsdb_compactions_failed_total` is increasing\n- Compaction logs show repeated errors or no log output\n\n---\n\n## 3. Failure Modes and Diagnostics\n\n### Failure Mode 1: Disk Space Exhaustion\n\n**Symptoms:**\n- Prometheus crashes or becomes unresponsive\n- `prometheus_tsdb_compactions_failed_total` increases\n- Logs show: `write block: ... mkdirAll ... no space left on device` or `I/O error`\n- Write operations rejected with \"disk full\" errors\n- Compaction metric `prometheus_tsdb_compaction_populating_block` remains at 1\n\n**Root Causes:**\n1. Retention policy allows blocks to accumulate beyond available disk space\n2. WAL (Write-Ahead Log) fills up unexpectedly (large batch of samples)\n3. Temporary block files (`.tmp-for-creation`) not cleaned up after failed compactions\n4. Block history grows faster than cleanup can remove old blocks\n5. Misconfigured `MaxBytes` or `RetentionDuration` exceeds available storage\n\n**Diagnostic Steps:**\n\n```bash\n# 1. Check disk space\ndf -h /path/to/prometheus/data\n\n# 2. Examine block directory sizes\ndu -sh /path/to/prometheus/data/tsdb/*/\ndu -sh /path/to/prometheus/data/wal\n\n# 3. Find orphaned temporary files\nfind /path/to/prometheus/data -name \"*.tmp-for-*\" -type d\n\n# 4. List all blocks with their sizes (requires promtool)\npromtool tsdb list --humanreadable /path/to/prometheus/data\n\n# 5. Check Prometheus logs for compaction errors\ngrep -i \"compact\\|disk\\|space\" /var/log/prometheus/prometheus.log | tail -50\n\n# 6. Verify retention configuration\n# Check prometheus.yml or check metrics:\n# - prometheus_tsdb_retention_limit_bytes\n# - prometheus_tsdb_retention_limit_seconds\n```\n\n**Code References:**\n- **Write Path**: `tsdb/compact.go:622-628` - Creates temporary block directory\n- **Sync Error Handling**: `tsdb/compact.go:702-704` - Syncs block to disk before rename\n- **Block Rotation**: `tsdb/db.go:1190` - \"Clear some disk space before compacting blocks\"\n\n---\n\n### Failure Mode 2: Compaction Stuck (Not Progressing)\n\n**Symptoms:**\n- Compaction counter `prometheus_tsdb_compactions_total` doesn't increase for >30 minutes\n- Head block grows indefinitely, consuming memory\n- Queries become slower as more blocks must be scanned\n- No compaction errors in logs, but no success messages either\n- `prometheus_tsdb_compaction_populating_block` stuck at 1\n\n**Root Causes:**\n1. Compaction mutex held by another operation (deadlock)\n2. Overlapping blocks causing repeated vertical compaction attempts\n3. Insufficient memory for chunk merging (OOM killer pauses process)\n4. I/O bottleneck: slow disks or network-mounted storage\n5. Compaction context canceled (e.g., during graceful shutdown)\n6. Auto-compaction disabled via `DisableCompactions()`\n\n**Diagnostic Steps:**\n\n```bash\n# 1. Check if compaction is disabled\n# Look for prometheus logs:\ngrep -i \"disable.*compact\" /var/log/prometheus/prometheus.log\n\n# 2. Monitor compaction loop activity\n# Watch for these in logs over 5 minutes:\ngrep \"compact blocks\\|compact head\\|write block\" /var/log/prometheus/prometheus.log | tail -20\n\n# 3. Check for overlapping blocks (triggers vertical compaction)\npromtool tsdb analyze --humanreadable /path/to/prometheus/data 2>&1 | head -50\n\n# 4. List blocks sorted by time to detect overlaps\npromtool tsdb list --humanreadable /path/to/prometheus/data | sort -k2\n\n# 5. Check system resources (memory, I/O)\nvmstat 1 5        # Check memory and swap usage\niostat -x 1 5     # Check disk I/O wait\n\n# 6. Check if Prometheus process is paused or stuck in I/O\nps aux | grep prometheus\nstrace -p <prometheus-pid> 2>&1 | head -50\n\n# 7. Look for pending sync operations\nlsof /path/to/prometheus/data | grep tmp-for-creation\n```\n\n**Code References:**\n- **Compaction Loop**: `tsdb/db.go:990-1027` - Main event loop with 1-minute ticker\n- **Compaction Mutex**: `tsdb/db.go:223-224` - `cmtx` prevents concurrent compactions\n- **Overlapping Detection**: `tsdb/compact.go:330-353` - `selectOverlappingDirs()`\n- **Context Cancellation**: `tsdb/compact.go:528-536` - Handles context cancellation during compaction\n\n---\n\n### Failure Mode 3: Block Corruption\n\n**Symptoms:**\n- Queries fail with: `cannot populate chunk ... checksum mismatch`\n- Prometheus logs: `invalid magic number` or `invalid segment header`\n- Specific blocks cannot be read; compaction skips them\n- `prometheus_tsdb_reloads_failures_total` increases\n- Block metadata shows inconsistent statistics\n\n**Root Causes:**\n1. Incomplete write during compaction (crash or power loss during `write()`)\n2. Bit flip or storage corruption (undetected by filesystem)\n3. Concurrent modifications to block files (race condition or external tampering)\n4. Index file corruption (index segments have checksums)\n5. Chunk segment corruption (each segment has CRC validation)\n6. Truncated WAL or block during replay\n\n**Diagnostic Steps:**\n\n```bash\n# 1. Identify the corrupted block\n# Extract ULID from error logs\ngrep -i \"checksum\\|invalid\\|corrupt\" /var/log/prometheus/prometheus.log | tail -20\n\n# 2. List all blocks and verify metadata\npromtool tsdb list --humanreadable /path/to/prometheus/data\n\n# 3. Attempt to analyze the problematic block (replace ULID)\npromtool tsdb analyze --humanreadable \\\n  /path/to/prometheus/data/tsdb/<ULID> 2>&1\n\n# 4. Check block structure\nls -la /path/to/prometheus/data/tsdb/<ULID>/\nfile /path/to/prometheus/data/tsdb/<ULID>/index\nfile /path/to/prometheus/data/tsdb/<ULID>/chunks/*\n\n# 5. Verify WAL integrity\nls -la /path/to/prometheus/data/wal/\n# Look for incomplete segments or .tmp files\n\n# 6. Check for recent file modifications\nstat /path/to/prometheus/data/tsdb/<ULID>/*\n```\n\n**Code References:**\n- **Index Validation**: `tsdb/index/index.go` - Index reader validates magic number and version\n- **Chunk Checksum**: `tsdb/chunks/chunks.go` - ChunkReader validates CRC on read\n- **Block Opening**: `tsdb/block.go:45-85` - `OpenBlock()` validates all components\n- **Corruption Detection**: `tsdb/block_test.go:92-186` - Test cases showing corruption patterns\n\n---\n\n### Failure Mode 4: Out-of-Memory (OOM) During Compaction\n\n**Symptoms:**\n- Prometheus killed by OOM or crashes during compaction\n- Logs show: `fatal error: runtime: out of memory` or similar\n- System shows increased memory usage just before crash\n- `prometheus_tsdb_compaction_populating_block` stuck at 1 before crash\n- Heap profile shows large spike in memory\n\n**Root Causes:**\n1. Very large blocks being merged simultaneously\n2. High cardinality metrics causing index explosion during merge\n3. Chunk pool exhaustion (all in-memory chunks held)\n4. Insufficient memory allocated to Prometheus (heap size too small)\n5. Memory leaks in index merging (symbol table duplication)\n6. Too many overlapping blocks requiring simultaneous loading\n\n**Diagnostic Steps:**\n\n```bash\n# 1. Check available memory and heap allocation\nfree -h\n# Find Prometheus process and check RSS, VSZ\nps aux | grep prometheus\n\n# 2. Monitor memory during compaction\n# In one terminal, watch memory:\nwatch -n 1 'ps aux | grep prometheus | grep -v grep'\n\n# 3. Enable pprof endpoints and collect heap profile\n# (if Prometheus has web UI on port 9090):\ncurl http://localhost:9090/debug/pprof/heap > heap_before.prof\n# Wait for compaction to start\nsleep 30\ncurl http://localhost:9090/debug/pprof/heap > heap_during.prof\n\n# 4. Check block cardinality (high cardinality = higher memory)\npromtool tsdb analyze \\\n  /path/to/prometheus/data/tsdb/<ULID> \\\n  --limit 10 \\\n  --extended 2>&1 | head -100\n\n# 5. Check configuration for memory limits\n# Review --storage.tsdb.* flags or prometheus.yml for:\n# - MaxBlockChunkSegmentSize (default 512MB)\n# - SamplesPerChunk (affects chunk count)\n\n# 6. Monitor page faults (swap usage)\nvmstat 1 10 | head -15\n```\n\n**Code References:**\n- **Chunk Pool**: `tsdb/chunkenc/pool.go` - Memory pool for chunks during compaction\n- **PopulateBlock**: `tsdb/compact.go:729-875` - Iterates through all series in all blocks\n- **Symbol Table Merging**: `tsdb/compact.go:800-810` - Merges symbol tables from multiple blocks\n- **Block Metadata**: `tsdb/db.go:204-206` - ChunkPool configuration\n\n---\n\n## 4. Recovery Procedures\n\n### Recovery for Failure Mode 1: Disk Space Exhaustion\n\n#### **Procedure 1A: Emergency Cleanup**\n\n**Risk Level**: Low | **Downtime**: <5 minutes\n\n1. **Stop Prometheus**\n   ```bash\n   systemctl stop prometheus\n   # or\n   kill <prometheus-pid>\n   ```\n\n2. **Remove oldest blocks to free space immediately**\n   ```bash\n   cd /path/to/prometheus/data/tsdb\n\n   # List blocks sorted by min time (oldest first)\n   ls -d */ | head -20\n\n   # Remove oldest 10% of blocks (be cautious)\n   # First, identify which blocks to delete:\n   ls -t -d */ | tail -5\n\n   # Remove them\n   for block in $(ls -t -d */ | tail -5); do\n     rm -rf \"$block\"\n   done\n   ```\n\n3. **Clean up temporary files**\n   ```bash\n   find /path/to/prometheus/data -name \"*.tmp-for-*\" -type d -exec rm -rf {} \\;\n   ```\n\n4. **Verify space freed**\n   ```bash\n   df -h /path/to/prometheus/data\n   du -sh /path/to/prometheus/data/tsdb\n   ```\n\n5. **Restart Prometheus**\n   ```bash\n   systemctl start prometheus\n   ```\n\n#### **Procedure 1B: Reduce Retention (Permanent Fix)**\n\n1. **Check current retention**\n   ```bash\n   # In prometheus.yml, look for:\n   global:\n     external_labels:\n       ...\n   # OR check startup flags for:\n   # --storage.tsdb.retention.time (e.g., 15d)\n   # --storage.tsdb.retention.size (e.g., 50GB)\n   ```\n\n2. **Edit Prometheus configuration**\n   ```yaml\n   # /etc/prometheus/prometheus.yml\n   global:\n     scrape_interval: 15s\n     # Reduce from 15d to 7d for example:\n\n   # Add or modify storage config:\n   storage:\n     tsdb:\n       retention:\n         time: 7d      # Changed from 15d\n         size: 30GB    # Optional: max bytes to keep\n   ```\n\n3. **Reload or restart Prometheus**\n   ```bash\n   # Option A: Reload config (no downtime)\n   kill -HUP <prometheus-pid>\n\n   # Option B: Restart (requires downtime)\n   systemctl restart prometheus\n   ```\n\n4. **Monitor for block deletion**\n   ```bash\n   # Watch logs for time retention:\n   tail -f /var/log/prometheus/prometheus.log | grep \"time_retentions_total\"\n   ```\n\n#### **Procedure 1C: Expand Storage (If Possible)**\n\n1. **Add a new disk or resize existing storage**\n   ```bash\n   # For cloud: Expand EBS/persistent disk\n   # For local: Add new disk and mount\n   sudo mkfs.ext4 /dev/sdb1\n   sudo mount /dev/sdb1 /mnt/prometheus-data-new\n   ```\n\n2. **Migrate data (while Prometheus is stopped)**\n   ```bash\n   systemctl stop prometheus\n   rsync -av /var/lib/prometheus/tsdb/ /mnt/prometheus-data-new/tsdb/\n   ```\n\n3. **Update Prometheus storage path** in systemd or config\n\n4. **Restart Prometheus**\n   ```bash\n   systemctl start prometheus\n   ```\n\n---\n\n### Recovery for Failure Mode 2: Compaction Stuck\n\n#### **Procedure 2A: Re-enable Auto-Compaction**\n\n**Risk Level**: Very Low | **Downtime**: 0 minutes\n\n1. **Check if compaction is disabled**\n   ```bash\n   # Search Prometheus logs\n   grep \"DisableCompactions\\|disabled\" /var/log/prometheus/prometheus.log\n\n   # Check if running with --storage.tsdb.no-lockfile (unrelated but note it)\n   ps aux | grep prometheus | grep storage\n   ```\n\n2. **If explicitly disabled, restart Prometheus normally**\n   ```bash\n   # If you disabled it via API or code, restart with default settings\n   systemctl restart prometheus\n   ```\n\n3. **Verify compaction resumes**\n   ```bash\n   # Watch for compaction in logs (every ~1-2 minutes)\n   tail -f /var/log/prometheus/prometheus.log | grep \"compact\"\n\n   # OR watch metrics\n   watch -n 5 'curl -s http://localhost:9090/api/v1/query?query=prometheus_tsdb_compactions_total | grep prometheus_tsdb_compactions_total'\n   ```\n\n#### **Procedure 2B: Force Reloadof Blocks and Retry Compaction**\n\n**Risk Level**: Low | **Downtime**: 0 minutes\n\n1. **Monitor current state**\n   ```bash\n   promtool tsdb list --humanreadable /path/to/prometheus/data | wc -l\n   # Note the number of blocks\n   ```\n\n2. **Send SIGHUP to reload blocks** (no downtime)\n   ```bash\n   kill -HUP <prometheus-pid>\n\n   # Verify in logs:\n   grep \"reloadBlocks\\|reloads_total\" /var/log/prometheus/prometheus.log | tail -5\n   ```\n\n3. **Monitor compaction progress**\n   ```bash\n   # Should see compaction attempts within 1 minute:\n   tail -f /var/log/prometheus/prometheus.log | grep -E \"compact|Compact\"\n   ```\n\n#### **Procedure 2C: Fix Overlapping Blocks**\n\n**Risk Level**: Medium | **Downtime**: <10 minutes\n\nIf overlapping blocks are detected and causing repeated vertical compaction attempts:\n\n1. **Identify overlapping blocks**\n   ```bash\n   promtool tsdb list --humanreadable /path/to/prometheus/data > /tmp/blocks.txt\n   cat /tmp/blocks.txt\n   # Look for blocks where next block's MIN TIME < previous block's MAX TIME\n   ```\n\n2. **Force manual compaction of overlaps**\n   ```bash\n   # Stop Prometheus\n   systemctl stop prometheus\n\n   # List blocks again to confirm overlap\n   promtool tsdb list --humanreadable /path/to/prometheus/data\n   ```\n\n3. **Use promtool to verify block integrity** (optional but recommended)\n   ```bash\n   promtool tsdb analyze --humanreadable \\\n     /path/to/prometheus/data/tsdb/<ULID1> 2>&1 | head -20\n   ```\n\n4. **Restart Prometheus** (it will compact on startup)\n   ```bash\n   systemctl start prometheus\n\n   # Monitor compaction logs\n   tail -f /var/log/prometheus/prometheus.log | grep -E \"compact|vertical\"\n   ```\n\n#### **Procedure 2D: Increase Memory or Optimize Configuration**\n\nIf compaction is stuck due to memory or resource limits:\n\n1. **Increase Prometheus heap**\n   ```bash\n   # Edit systemd service or startup script\n   sudo systemctl edit prometheus\n\n   # Add or modify:\n   [Service]\n   Environment=\"GOGC=75\"\n   Environment=\"GOMAXPROCS=4\"\n\n   # OR via JVM equivalent (if using Java Prometheus):\n   # -Xmx16g -Xms16g\n   ```\n\n2. **Optimize compaction configuration** in `prometheus.yml`\n   ```yaml\n   storage:\n     tsdb:\n       # Reduce max block size (less memory per merge)\n       max-block-duration: 2h\n\n       # Increase min block duration to reduce compaction frequency\n       min-block-duration: 2h\n\n       # Reduce samples per chunk (more chunks, less memory per chunk)\n       samples-per-chunk: 4096  # default\n   ```\n\n3. **Restart Prometheus**\n   ```bash\n   systemctl restart prometheus\n   ```\n\n---\n\n### Recovery for Failure Mode 3: Block Corruption\n\n#### **Procedure 3A: Delete Corrupted Block (Data Loss)**\n\n**Risk Level**: High (data loss) | **Downtime**: <5 minutes\n\n⚠️ **Warning**: This procedure results in loss of that block's data.\n\n1. **Identify corrupted block from logs**\n   ```bash\n   # Extract ULID from error message\n   grep -i \"checksum\\|invalid\" /var/log/prometheus/prometheus.log | grep -o \"[0-9A-Z]\\{26\\}\"\n   ```\n\n2. **Confirm block is corrupted**\n   ```bash\n   ULID=\"<extracted-ulid>\"\n   promtool tsdb analyze --humanreadable /path/to/prometheus/data/tsdb/$ULID 2>&1\n   # Should show errors\n   ```\n\n3. **Stop Prometheus**\n   ```bash\n   systemctl stop prometheus\n   ```\n\n4. **Backup and delete the block**\n   ```bash\n   ULID=\"<extracted-ulid>\"\n   tar -czf /backup/corrupted-block-$ULID.tar.gz /path/to/prometheus/data/tsdb/$ULID\n   rm -rf /path/to/prometheus/data/tsdb/$ULID\n   ```\n\n5. **Restart Prometheus**\n   ```bash\n   systemctl start prometheus\n\n   # Verify it starts without errors\n   sleep 5\n   tail /var/log/prometheus/prometheus.log\n   ```\n\n6. **Re-scrape lost data** (optional)\n   - If you have remote storage or can re-backfill, do so now\n   - Future scrapes will fill in the gap\n\n#### **Procedure 3B: Rebuild Block from WAL** (If possible)\n\n**Risk Level**: Low | **Downtime**: 5-30 minutes (depending on WAL size)\n\nIf corruption occurred during compaction but WAL is intact:\n\n1. **Stop Prometheus**\n   ```bash\n   systemctl stop prometheus\n   ```\n\n2. **Flush WAL to a new block**\n   ```bash\n   # Use promtool to extract WAL\n   promtool tsdb dump /path/to/prometheus/data > /tmp/tsdb_dump.txt\n\n   # This creates a temporary block from WAL data\n   # Alternative: Delete the corrupted block and let Prometheus replay WAL on restart\n   ```\n\n3. **Delete corrupted block**\n   ```bash\n   rm -rf /path/to/prometheus/data/tsdb/<ULID>\n   ```\n\n4. **Restart Prometheus** (WAL will be replayed)\n   ```bash\n   systemctl start prometheus\n   ```\n\n#### **Procedure 3C: Restore from Backup**\n\n**Risk Level**: Low | **Downtime**: Depends on backup size\n\nIf you have recent backups:\n\n1. **Stop Prometheus**\n   ```bash\n   systemctl stop prometheus\n   ```\n\n2. **Restore from backup**\n   ```bash\n   # Assuming you have daily backups\n   tar -xzf /backups/prometheus-tsdb-$(date -d yesterday +%Y%m%d).tar.gz \\\n     -C /path/to/prometheus/data\n   ```\n\n3. **Restart Prometheus**\n   ```bash\n   systemctl start prometheus\n   ```\n\n---\n\n### Recovery for Failure Mode 4: Out-of-Memory (OOM)\n\n#### **Procedure 4A: Increase Memory Allocation**\n\n**Risk Level**: Low | **Downtime**: <5 minutes\n\n1. **Identify current memory allocation**\n   ```bash\n   # Check systemd service\n   systemctl cat prometheus | grep -E \"Memory|GOMAXPROCS\"\n\n   # Check running process\n   ps aux | grep prometheus | grep -v grep\n   ```\n\n2. **Increase memory limit (systemd)**\n   ```bash\n   sudo systemctl edit prometheus\n\n   # Add or modify:\n   [Service]\n   MemoryAccounting=true\n   MemoryLimit=20G\n   MemoryMax=24G\n   ```\n\n3. **Increase GOGC (Go garbage collection) to be less aggressive**\n   ```bash\n   sudo systemctl edit prometheus\n\n   [Service]\n   Environment=\"GOGC=100\"  # Default 100; higher = less frequent GC, more memory\n   ```\n\n4. **Restart Prometheus**\n   ```bash\n   systemctl restart prometheus\n   ```\n\n#### **Procedure 4B: Reduce Block Merge Concurrency**\n\n**Risk Level**: Very Low (slightly slower compaction) | **Downtime**: 0 minutes\n\n1. **Edit Prometheus configuration**\n   ```yaml\n   storage:\n     tsdb:\n       # Reduce max merging blocks (compacts fewer blocks at once)\n       # Note: Prometheus merges up to 3 blocks by default\n       # You may need to rebuild if this is configurable\n\n       # Workaround: Increase time window to compact less frequently\n       max-block-duration: 4h  # Default 2h; higher = bigger blocks, fewer merges\n       min-block-duration: 4h\n   ```\n\n2. **Reload or restart**\n   ```bash\n   kill -HUP <prometheus-pid>  # Reload (if config hot-reload supported)\n   # OR\n   systemctl restart prometheus\n   ```\n\n#### **Procedure 4C: Reduce Cardinality (Long-term Fix)**\n\n**Risk Level**: Low | **Downtime**: 0 minutes\n\nHigh cardinality metrics require more memory during index merging:\n\n1. **Identify high-cardinality metrics**\n   ```bash\n   promtool tsdb analyze /path/to/prometheus/data/tsdb/<ULID> --limit 5\n\n   # Look for metrics with many unique label combinations\n   ```\n\n2. **Reduce cardinality in scrape configs**\n   ```yaml\n   scrape_configs:\n     - job_name: 'my-job'\n       relabeling:\n         # Drop high-cardinality labels\n         - source_labels: [__meta_kubernetes_pod_uid]\n           action: drop  # Don't keep this label\n   ```\n\n3. **Restart Prometheus**\n   ```bash\n   systemctl restart prometheus\n   ```\n\n---\n\n## 5. 1133-1236 | Orchestrates head + block compaction |\n| `compactBlocks()` | `tsdb/db.go` | 1357-1393 | Iteratively compacts all eligible blocks |\n| `compactHead()` | `tsdb/db.go` | 1334-1352 | Flushes compaction |\n\n### Error Handling Paths\n\n| Error Scenario | Handler | Code |\n|---|---|---|\n| Disk full during write | Deferred cleanup in `write()` | `tsdb/compact.go:611-617` |\n| Context cancelled mid-compaction | Multi-error collector | `tsdb/compact.go:527-536` |\n| Block open failure | Error logged, block marked failed | `tsdb/compact.go:475-479` |\n| Tombstone write failure | Logged but compaction continues | `tsdb/compact.go:688-690` |\n| Metadata write failure | Returns error, tmp dir cleaned | `tsdb/compact.go:683-685` |\n| Chunk write failure | Rolled back, block marked failed | `tsdb/compact.go:850-852` |\n\n### Monitoring Integration\n\n| Metric Update | Code | Trigger |\n|---|---|---|\n| `prometheus_tsdb_compactions_total` | `tsdb/compact.go:618` | Every compaction attempt (deferred) |\n| `prometheus_tsdb_compaction_duration_seconds` | `tsdb/compact.go:619` | Compaction completes (success or failure) |\n| `prometheus_tsdb_vertical_compactions_total` | `tsdb/compact.go:760` | Overlapping blocks detected during merge |\n| `prometheus_tsdb_compaction_populating_block` | `tsdb/compact.go:748, 746` | Set to 1 at start, 0 at end of PopulateBlock |\n| `prometheus_tsdb_compactions_failed_total` | `tsdb/db.go:1014` | Compaction returns error |\n| `prometheus_tsdb_compactions_triggered_total` | `tsdb/db.go:1009` | Compaction loop receives signal |\n\n---\n\n## 6. Quick Reference: promtool Commands\n\n### Viewing Block Information\n\n```bash\n# List all blocks with human-readable output\npromtool tsdb list --humanreadable /path/to/prometheus/data\n\n# Analyze a specific block (high cardinality, churn, etc.)\npromtool tsdb analyze --humanreadable /path/to/prometheus/data/tsdb/<ULID>\n\n# Dump all samples from a block\npromtool tsdb dump /path/to/prometheus/data/tsdb/<ULID> > dump.txt\n\n# Export block as OpenMetrics format\npromtool tsdb dump-openmetrics /path/to/prometheus/data\n```\n\n### Benchmarking and Testing\n\n```bash\n# Run write performance benchmark\npromtool tsdb bench write --out=/tmp/tsdb-bench --num-metrics 100000\n\n# Analyze churn and compaction efficiency\npromtool tsdb analyze /path/to/prometheus/data --extended\n```\n\n---\n\n## 7. Prevention Best Practices\n\n1. **Set reasonable retention policies**: Don't set `retention.time` or `retention.size` based on available disk; leave 30% headroom for temporary files during compaction.\n\n2. **Monitor proactively**: Set up the alert rules in section 2 to catch issues early.\n\n3. **Regular backups**: Daily snapshots of `/path/to/prometheus/data/tsdb` to enable quick recovery from corruption.\n\n4. **Capacity planning**: Estimate growth as `(samples/sec) × 1 month`, multiply by retention, and provision 1.5× that space.\n\n5. **Resource allocation**: Allocate at least 25% of system memory to Prometheus to avoid OOM during large compactions.\n\n6. **Upgrade regularly**: Keep Prometheus updated to get compaction improvements and bug fixes.\n\n7. **Test recovery**: Periodically simulate failures and practice recovery procedures to ensure your team is prepared.\n\n---\n\n## 8. Appendix: Configuration Reference\n\n### Key Configuration Options Affecting Compaction\n\n```yaml\n# prometheus.yml global section\nglobal:\n  scrape_interval: 15s\n\n# Storage configuration\nstorage:\n  tsdb:\n    # Retention time (default: 15d)\n    retention:\n      time: 7d\n\n      # OR Max bytes (optional, default: disabled)\n      size: 50GB\n\n    # Block duration ranges\n    min-block-duration: 2h\n    max-block-duration: 2h\n\n    # Chunk configuration (affects memory during compaction)\n    samples-per-chunk: 4096\n\n    # WAL configuration\n    wal-compression: none  # or 'snappy'\n    wal-segment-size: 128MB\n\n    # Out-of-order support\n    out-of-order-time-window: 0  # Disable OOO; >0 enables it\n```\n\n### Prometheus Startup Flags\n\n```bash\nprometheus \\\n  --storage.tsdb.path=/var/lib/prometheus/tsdb \\\n  --storage.tsdb.retention.time=7d \\\n  --storage.tsdb.retention.size=50GB \\\n  --storage.tsdb.max-block-duration=2h \\\n  --storage.tsdb.min-block-duration=2h \\\n  --query.max-samples=10000000\n```\n\n---\n\n**Document Version**: 1.0 | **Last Updated**: 2024 | **Status**: Ready for Production\n","structuredPatch":[],"originalFile":null}}

{"type":"user","message":{"role":"user","content":[{"tool_use_id":"toolu_0129ikGw12XxbPpUbCwdBGP1","type":"tool_result","content":"# Prometheus TSDB Compaction - Operational Runbook\n\n## 1. Overview\n\n### What is TSDB Compaction?\n\nTSDB (Time Series Database) compaction is a critical background process that merges overlapping time series blocks, removes deleted series via tombstones, and maintains efficient query performance over time. The compaction process transforms raw data written from the WAL (Write-Ahead Log) into optimized, hierarchical block structures.\n\n### Why Compaction is Needed\n\n- **Performance**: Reduces the number of blocks queried, improving query latency\n- **Disk Efficiency**: Merges small blocks into larger ones, reducing index overhead\n- **Cleanup**: Removes tombstoned (deleted) series, recovering disk space\n- **Query Optimization**: Creates higher-level blocks that cover longer time ranges\n\n### Block Structure and Compaction Levels\n\nPrometheus uses a **leveled compaction strategy** where blocks are organized hierarchically:\n\n- **Level 0 (Head Block)**: Data currently being written. Not yet compacted.\n- **Level 1+**: Progressively larger blocks created by merging Level N-1 blocks.\n\nBlock ranges follow an exponential progression (default: 2h, 10h, 50h, 250h, ...). Each time a set of blocks is merged, the compaction level increases.\n\n**Compaction Metadata** (`meta.json` in each block):\n- `Compaction.Level`: Indicates how many times this block has been compacted\n- `Compaction.Sources`: Original block ULIDs that contributed to this block\n- `Compaction.Parents`: Direct parent blocks merged to create this block\n- `Stats.NumTombstones`: Count of deleted series in the block\n\n### When Compaction is Triggered\n\nCompaction occurs through **two mechanisms**:\n\n#### 1. **Time-Based Triggering**\n- **Primary Trigger**: Every 1 minute, a compaction check is run\n- **Head Compaction**: When the head block spans > 1.5× the configured chunk range (default: 2 hours)\n- **Block Selection**: The compaction planner examines all blocks and selects eligible groups for merging\n\n#### 2. **Size-Based Triggering**\n- **High Tombstone Rate**: Blocks with >5% tombstones are compacted to remove deleted series\n- **Full Block Deletion**: If a block consists entirely of tombstoned series (NumTombstones ≥ NumSeries), it's compacted immediately\n- **Overlapping Blocks**: If blocks overlap in time, vertical compaction merges them to maintain a clean time structure\n\n#### Code Reference\n- **Trigger Loop**: `tsdb/db.go:990-1027` - Main compaction loop running every 1 minute\n- **Compaction Planner**: `tsdb/compact.go:222-286` - `Plan()` determines blocks for compaction\n- **Head Compactability**: `tsdb/head.go:1633-1639` - Checks if head is ready to be compacted\n- **Block Selection**: `tsdb/compact.go:289-326` - `selectDirs()` groups blocks by time range\n\n---\n\n## 2. Monitoring Indicators\n\n### Key Prometheus Metrics\n\nMonitor these metrics in your Prometheus installation to track compaction health:\n\n#### **Primary Compaction Metrics**\n\n| Metric | Type | Description | Alert Threshold |\n|--------|------|-------------|-----------------|\n| `prometheus_tsdb_compactions_total` | Counter | Total successful compactions executed | None (informational) |\n| `prometheus_tsdb_compaction_duration_seconds` | Histogram | Time taken per compaction run | p95 > 5m indicates slow compaction |\n| `prometheus_tsdb_vertical_compactions_total` | Counter | Count of overlapping block compactions | Rapid increases suggest data overlap issues |\n| `prometheus_tsdb_compaction_populating_block` | Gauge | Set to 1 while writing a block to disk | >60s suggests I/O bottleneck or memory pressure |\n| `prometheus_tsdb_compactions_triggered_total` | Counter | Compactions initiated by planner | Should track with `compactions_total` |\n| `prometheus_tsdb_compactions_failed_total` | Counter | Compactions that failed | **ALERT if > 0** (critical) |\n| `prometheus_tsdb_compactions_skipped_total` | Counter | Skipped due to `DisableCompactions()` | Normal if intentional |\n\n#### **Supplementary Metrics**\n\n| Metric | Type | Description | Alert Threshold |\n|--------|------|-------------|-----------------|\n| `prometheus_tsdb_blocks_loaded` | Gauge | Currently loaded block count | >500 blocks indicates poor compaction |\n| `prometheus_tsdb_storage_blocks_bytes` | Gauge | Total bytes in all loaded blocks | Compare with `retention_limit_bytes` |\n| `prometheus_tsdb_retention_limit_bytes` | Gauge | Max bytes configured for retention | N/A |\n| `prometheus_tsdb_tombstone_cleanup_seconds` | Histogram | Time to recompact blocks for tombstone removal | p95 > 2m indicates issue |\n\n#### **Chunk Metrics** (Level 1 compactions only)\n\n| Metric | Type | Description | Use Case |\n|--------|------|-------------|----------|\n| `prometheus_tsdb_compaction_chunk_size_bytes` | Histogram | Size of chunks written | Detect anomalously large/small chunks |\n| `prometheus_tsdb_compaction_chunk_samples` | Histogram | Samples per chunk during compaction | p95 should align with `SamplesPerChunk` config |\n| `prometheus_tsdb_compaction_chunk_range_seconds` | Histogram | Time span of chunks | Verify chunks align with block ranges |\n\n### Alert Rules\n\n```yaml\ngroups:\n  - name: PrometheusCompaction\n    rules:\n      # Critical: Compaction is failing\n
